==Introduction==

=--Our goal to you, the reader...--=
|+3|
||c '' ...is to make sure that you are able to get a perfect game, meaning that you can find all of the items, explore all of the areas, uncover anything that is hidden, and see all there is to see. '' ||
|+3|
=-=

For this guide, we have decided to create an extensive FAQ/Walkthrough. The walkthrough is the main focus; it walks you through the whole game step-by-step, leading you to the locations of all of the items in the game, strategies for fighting the bosses, and even walking you through the miscellaneous extras thrown your way in the game. It will also be an extensive FAQ, which includes lists of all of the items, equipment, etc., as well as a complete bestiary.

+
+
+
+

==Starting Up==
Before even starting the game, there are a few things you should probably take a look at, just to be safe.

+
+
+

=--Note... (DLC)--=
Before starting your game, make sure to stop by the PlayStation Store to pick up a couple of freebies, or even drop some dough to start off comfortably! Make sure to at least get the three freebies to start off with some extra cash, costumes, and materials!

Oh, and don't forget to activate any DLC you received with the Limited Edition copy! (Not only do they change the costumes, but they change the characters' battle themes to those of their respective games.)

*Purchased items will be automatically installed upon boot-up of the game.
*Access the Downloadable Content section (right most header) of the Items Menu to unlock purchase.

+

'''''For the gald and Level Up DLC...'''''
*This can only be utilized once per playthrough, and cannot be reversed upon activation.
*Excess over the maximum capacity will be discarded upon use.
*The DLC pack cannot be utilized if player has already reached the maximum amount.

+

'''''For the Costume DLC...'''''
*Scroll down to the Attachments section of the Equipment Menu to equip costumes and attachments.
*Equipped attachments can be modified by pressing the START button in the Attachments section of the equipment Menu.
=-=

+
+
+

===Controls===
^l2|

^l3|

+
+
+

===Character Selection===

After setting all of your options and watching the intro movies, you'll need to choose your main character. The story is very much the same for both; there are just small differences between Jude's and Milla's viewpoints at certain points of the story, and you only see the viewpoint of the character you control; if they're separated, you'll see what the other did not. The only other major difference is that a different battle theme plays depending on your character; I believe Jude's is far better.

^sl4|

%

A kind, clever medical student who left home to attend school in the capital city. Poised to graduate, Jude is eager to find his purpose in life.

If you choose Jude, then start following along here: [[Jude's Beginning]]

^sr5|

%

A mysterious young woman accompanied by four unseen beings. She comes across as calm, collected, and wise beyond her years.

If you choose Milla, then start following along here: [[Milla's Beginning]]

%

+
+
+
+

==Chapter 1==

The story starts here in Fennmont! Even though there are two different characters, as stated before, a playthrough will be very similar. Notes will be included throughout the walkthrough to let you know when something character-specific needs to be made known.

=--Note...--=
Press R1 (the Navi Button) on the field to view your current objective. You can also check your current objective or read a detailed synopsis of the story from the Event List on the menu.

Also, keep in mind that you can Quick Save anywhere; you can only store one Quick Save file at a time, so be sure to use Memory Rings regularly when you come across them for multiple saves.
=-=

+
+
+

===Jude's Beginning===

+

====Fennmont, Spirit-lit Seat of Kings====

^l6|
^l7|

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures      |
|c   [_] |c '' [[Orange Gel]]        '' |
|c   [_] |c '' [[Class Credit Form]] '' |
|c   [_] |c '' [[Life Bottle]]       '' |
|c   [_] |c '' [[100 gald]]          '' |
|c   [_] |c '' [[Apple Gel]]         '' |

+

|* Talim Medical School |

From the start here in the '''Teaching Wing''', head west just a bit to find a row of lockers; examine the left side of them to find '''''[[Orange Gel]]'''''. Feel free to talk to the NPC's around here (though it is a bit odd not to be able to talk to everyone; just the ones with smileys above their heads; the smileys will have open mouths if you haven't talked to them yet, and close mouths if you have), then make your way east to the '''Student Services''' area. Nothing of note in here, so continue outside. You can press SQUARE to see your map and all the places you can go, but for now, you can only head north and enter the '''Reception''' area to your west.

After a quick scene, you'll receive the '''''[[Class Credit Form]]'''''. Head southwest into the '''Outpatient Wing''', then move to the end of the hall to '''Examination Room 5''' to advance the story. After the scene, go back into the Examination Room and check the desk for a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''', then leave the building to be on our way to find Professor Haus. You can explore a bit more now -- but not by much.

Return to the '''Student Services''' building, and you should see a man sitting in a chair just to the east of the entrance. He should have a green (!) above his head; this signifies a Sub Event, so talk to him to unlock your first one: '''''[[The Cycle of Rieze Maxia]]'''''. Make sure to check out all Sub Events as you go along for more tidbits to the story, as well as shots at some Titles! From there, continue back to the '''Teaching Wing''' where you first started to find another Sub Event: '''''[[Rumors About Jude]]'''''. Once you've seen both Sub Events, head back outside to the three-way split to the east and take the southeastern path to the '''Central Plaza'''. Note the Memory Rings as you come across them; save often, and in different files, just to be safe.

First, make your way northwest and into the '''Hotel Fenntasia - Lobby'''. Ride the elevators at the end of the hall to the '''3F Hallway''' and check both rooms up here. '''Room 302''' has '''''[[100 gald]]''''' in an urn beside the door, and '''Room 303''' has '''''[[Apple Gel]]''''' in the dresser beside the bed. Return to the Plaza and move southwest next, entering the '''Samsara Trading Post 1F'''; it is here where you'll find all of the shops in one handy place! (Don't worry about buying anything though; the money will be better used later, and we'll also find/acquire these items soon enough anyway.)

Head back out to the Plaza and continue south to the '''Research District'''. Here, you'll find another Sub Event just to your west: '''''[[Spiritual Arte Failure]]'''''. Afterward, continue following along the path to the southwest for a scene with the guards. Start heading back toward the school for another scene, and you'll be inside the '''Laforte Research Center - Sewer Tunnel 1'''.

=--Note...--=
Even though the next section is titled 'Milla's Beginning', continue reading anyway; if you're playing as Jude, this section will still apply to you, as this is where the two stories merge. From here on out, anything Jude or Milla specific will be pointed out.
=-=

+
+
+

===Milla's Beginning===

+

====Laforte Research Center====

|c '''''[[Enemy Book]]'''''                 |

+

|* Sewer Tunnels |

=--Note...--=
# As you explore dungeons and towns throughout the game, you will come across sparkling/twinkling points, as well of bags of loot. These things will give you a random item/material/gald/etc., and will also appear somewhat randomly; sometimes they appear, sometimes they do not. Because of the randomness of these items, they will not be covered in the walkthrough; just be sure to keep an eye out for them as you explore.
# Obsessed with skits? Don't use any Gels till you get to Xian Du. Recommended for NG+ only.
=-=

In the northernmost part of the "H" hallway you're in is a chest containing '''''[[Cape]]''''', so be sure to grab it before proceeding to '''Sewer Tunnel 2'''. In this area, you will find your first battle; you can skip the tutorial if you like, which is a blessing to any Tales veteran; otherwise, pay close attention to learn the basics. After the battle, carry on to the next Sewer Tunnel (3 for Milla, 4 for Jude.) At the end of the area, you'll have another fight and tutorial. Afterward, climb the nearby ladder to '''Sector 2'''.

|* Sector 2 |

Near the door in the easternmost corner is a chest containing '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2'''''. From there, climb the stairs to the elevated central corridor and continue northwest; in the octagon-shaped structure up the stairs is a chest full of '''''[[Apple Gel]] x3'''''. Use the nearby Memory Ring, then climb the smaller stairs beside the Memory Ring itself. Continue through the northern door for a scene and your first boss battle.

+
+
+

%
====BOSS BATTLE #01====
@r|nZU5eWdiQ4k
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Girl in Red]]'''''                                           '''(LV. 05)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |

|c ''Normal''             |r   3000 |r       161 |r       196 |r       169 |r       159 |
|c ''Moderate''           |r   4500 |r       192 |r       234 |r       202 |r       191 |
|c ''Hard''               |r   7500 |r       241 |r       294 |r       253 |r       239 |

|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Wind                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Earth                                                     |

''Part 1:'' This part is for Jude only, leading to it being a two part battle. This first battle you're meant to lose, so go ahead and let her take you out (unless you want a lengthy, meaningless challenge.) The second part of the battle is fought by both regardless of who you're controlling.

''Part 2:'' Milla is super overpowered. Unless you're on a harder difficulty, even if Red staggers you a lot, there shouldn't be a problem mopping the floor with her. If you're not already controlling her, just use L1 and her directional button to take control of her, then spam Sylph or Undine using LEFT STICK + UP (or + RIGHT) to wipe her out. Hopefully you're quick enough and Jude wins some EXP as well.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |
|c     250 |c      500 |
+
|c ''' If you need additional help, watch this boss fight on YouTube using the link below, or through the embedded video above! ''' |
|c ''  http://youtu.be/nZU5eWdiQ4k                                                                                               '' |
|c ''' Video provided by ''' --- OmegaEvolution --- ''''' (videos may contain spoilers!) '''                                                    '' |
=-=
%


+
+
+

You will get the '''''[[Research Center Key]]''''', as well as the Title '''Research Center Intruder''' after the battle.

=--Note...--=
For those playing Milla, you will receive the '''''[[Enemy Book]]''''' and '''''[[Item Book]]''''' as well.
=-=

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** Laboratory 08: '''''[[Still Shaking]]''''', '''''[[Next Order of Business]]'''''
** Sector 2: '''''[[One and the Same]]''''', '''''[[Proof of Identity]]'''''
** Sector 3: '''''[[Cold Comfort]]''''', '''''[[Going Deeper]]''''', '''''[[Sparring Time]]'''''
+

Leave the room for another tutorial about Lilium Orbs. Feel free to develop the grid however you like, as it's pretty flexible! A Backdated Future pretty much leans toward building the STR and HP to begin with, but stays within the beginning levels of the grid to keep them balanced as he goes. Once he get the first two levels done, he goes outward to the third level, then the fourth and so on. You can also Auto-Level by pressing SELECT; if you don't want to put much thought into it and worry about other aspects of the game, then go ahead and do this. Drache took this lazy approach and she's a happier person for it. :D Do you want to be a happy person?

When you regain control, open the chest to the south for a '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''. Enter the room '''Laboratory 06''' to claim a '''''[[Chamomile]]''''' up the ladder. Leave, head downstairs and toward the door at the northwest end of the room to reach '''Sector 3'''.

|* Sector 3 |

The far western corner near the octagon-shaped platform has a chest containing '''''[[400 gald]]''''' end. Do not enter the nearest door to the east yet; you will miss some items. Instead, go up the stairs to the central corridor, then continue up the smaller set that lead up to the next level to the southeast. Enter '''Laboratory 12''' and climb the ladder inside for a chest containing '''''[[500 gald]]'''''. To the far northeast, open the two chests to the northeast for '''''[[Apple Gel]] x2''''' and '''''[[Orange Gel]]'''''. Now, head for the first door you ignored back on the ground floor along the southeastern wall, '''Laboratory 04''' for a scene...

And finally, the game's opening! Progress! Milla has now been nerfed, but we're sure you figured that out. :) Her skills are also vastly different.

|* Fennmont |

=--Note...--=
If you're playing as Milla, you'll acquire the '''''[[Kresnik Key]]''''' automatically.
=-=

There's nothing to do here after the battle, so continue to the next screen. The red dots on the map are enemies you can fight, and green ones are people you can talk to, so feel free to fight/chat. When you're ready, you need to go to the Seahaven, so head north to the '''Talim Medical School'''. As Jude suggested, head toward the eastern exit to reach '''Fennmont Seahaven'''. Watch the series of events, and you'll eventually regain control in the Aladhi Seahaven.

+
+
+

===Aladhi Seahaven / Trail===

^l9|

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures           |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries         |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]]          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Prickle Spider]]  '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]]            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Wolf]]            '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[600 gald]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Goblin]]          '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Saffron]]              '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Merfish]] (SE)    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Weird Fragment]] x4    '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Crab Man]] (SE)   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Boots]]                '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Axe Beak]] (SE)   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Item Sphere]]          '' |c-5 [_] |c-5 '' [[Fleet Mare]] (SE) '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[2000 gald]]            '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Wood Chunk]] x10       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]] x2         '' |
+
|* Alvin - Starting Equipment             |
|c '''''[[Broadsword]]'''''               |
|c '''''[[Leather Helm]]'''''             |
|c '''''[[Hard Mail]]'''''                |
|c '''''[[Normal Hairstyle (Alvin)]]''''' |
|c '''''[[Normal Attire (Alvin)]]'''''    |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[The Calamity Key]]''''', '''''[[Witness for the Defense]]'''''
+

You are introduced to Sub Events as you arrive; anyone with a green (!) icon will have something for you to do (if you're playing as Jude, you've already done a few.) Right in front of you is one such person; talk to her to proceed the story. (Rather than actually unlocking a Sub Event, this continues the main event.) Feel free to check out the shops while you're here as well, if you'd like to upgrade your equipment.

=--Note...--=
To unlock more items in the shops, you need to increase your shop level. This normally rises along with just shopping, but you can also either contribute gald or donate materials to the shops to earn points towards higher levels in a quicker fashion. Some shops will give you a bonus depending on the type of materials you donate to them. The higher the shop level, the better quality goods you can buy, and the cheaper the items will get.

For donating to increase the level, if you plan to donate materials, then it's probably best to wait until you've completed the Sub Events in the area, just in case you are asked for a material that may not come by very easily. This next area is handled quite easily with your default equipment, so you may want to wait until your return.
=-=

Once you're ready, head northeast to the '''Aladhi Trail'''.

^l10|

|* Aladhi Trail - South Region |

You'll be introduced to Linking upon arrival. When you regain control, make your way north and east for a forced skit ('''''[[There's a Town Around Here]]'''''). Continue hugging the eastern wall for a chest containing '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''. Since you can't continue in this direction, follow the northern wall back west. By the two trees southwest of there is a chest containing '''''[[Apple Gel]]'''''. From there, continue northwest and look for a chest in an alcove to the northeast for '''''[[600 gald]]'''''. Continue northwest to the next area.

|* Aladhi Trail - West Branch |

Follow along the northern wall, and you'll reach a chest containing '''''[[Saffron]]''''' in the shadow of trees at the western end of this section. Make your way back east, then as the path narrows to the south, look for a chest along the eastern wall next to a tree for '''''[[Weird Fragment]] x4'''''. Once you have that, continue along the southern path until you reach a dead-end with the monsters we were looking for. Don't worry; it's just another tutorial battle; this one is for Over Limit.

Afterward, check the chest directly ahead of you for some '''''[[Boots]]'''''; be sure to equip them on someone. When you're ready, head back to the '''Seahaven'''.

|* Aladhi Seahaven |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** Aladhi Seahaven - '''''[[Intelligence Work]]''''', '''''[[Creeping Suspicion]]'''''
** Aladhi Trail - South Region - '''''[[The Four]]''''', '''''[[Partners in Clime]]''''', '''''[[Alvin's Arsenal]]'''''
** Etc. '''''[[Inside and Out]]''''', '''''[[The Fundamentals of Combat]]''''', '''''[[Of Monster Bondage]]''''', '''''[[Mercenary Wisdom]]'''''
+

=--Note...--=
# Now that you can use Auto Items... don't turn them off! It can definitely be annoying to have your Apple Gels get eaten, but there is a trophy attached to 400 auto item uses.
# Make sure that your AI allies activate their skills (Jude's Restore, Milla's Bind, Alvin's Breaker) 150 times for a series of trophies. This one can take a while, so make sure to link with everyone from time to time.
# As the player, use each character's special skills (Snap Pivot, Spirit Shift, Charge) 150 times for even more trophies.
# For pretty much any trophy you can get, there is a title that demands a higher number. There are no trophies attached to getting all titles, so don't feel obligated to, for instance, Snap Pivot 450 times.
# Once you can buy food, never fight without it again. You need 800 encounters and you need to consume food 800 times, both for trophies.
# Shop levels max out at 100. Yep, that's another trophy.
=-=

Head back and talk to the client for an '''''[[Item Sphere]]''''' and '''''[[2000 gald]]'''''. Head to the inn; after the scene, you'll finally be able to buy from the Food Vendor. Food lasts several battles, at least, so you don't need to totally break the bank to buy a bunch (...though you can only have one of each food item). Do increase the shop levels often so you can get more items and discounts.

Head to the town's exit to get Alvin back. Now it's time for more sub events! Right behind you to the southwest are two clients for the Sub Events [[The Legendary Flavor]] and [[The Monster Lies]]. A third client, located at the northern tip of the area, is attached to [[Fruit Seller]]. Please click the links if you need help with those events. Remember to return to clients after you've killed monsters to reap your rewards. (You have to proceed before getting a Porange, so don't worry about the fruit yet for the last Sub Event.) Just head to the trail.

|* Aladhi Trail - South Region |

The path to the northeast is clear now, so unless you want to bash in monster skulls, proceed that way to the next area.

|* Aladhi Trail - North Region |

As you come to the split path just to the north, look just to the left of the large rock formation for a chest with '''''[[Wood Chunk]] x10'''''. From there, head all the way east for a chest containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''''', then continue north along the eastern wall to find another chest, this one with '''''[[Apple Gel]] x2'''''. After exploring the rest of the area for fights and extra random treasures, make your way to the far north to arrive in the next town, '''Hamil'''.

+
+
+

===Hamil, Orchard Frontier===

^l11|

|*+2 Hamil                                |*+4 Galia Trail                                                                   |
|c+2 '' Items / Equipment / Treasures  '' |c+2 '' Items / Equipment / Treasures ''     |c+2 '' Monster / Bestiary Entries '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Mysterious Jewel]]  '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[900 gald]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fleet Mare]]    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Napple]]            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Bandage]]              '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Insect Plant]]  '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Wild Bird Egg]] x3  '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]]          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Axe Beak]]      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[300 gald]]          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Orange Gel]] x2        '' |c-5 [_] |c-5 '' [[Tortoise]]      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]]         '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Pudding Cake (Small)]] '' |
|c-3 [_] |c-3 '' [[Life Bottle]]       '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Stun Bracelet]]        '' |
                                          |c   [_] |c   '' [[2000 gald]]            '' |
                                          |c   [_] |c   '' [[Orange Gel]]           '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[The Perfect Catalyst]]'''''
** ETC - '''''[[Echo]]''''', '''''[[Fruit of Temptation]]'''''
** At Galia Trail: '''''[[A Strange Girl]]''''', '''''[[Rashugal and Auj Oule]]'''''
+

=--Note...--=
The random junk you find in drawers and nightstands? Yeah, that counts as a treasure chest by the in-game counter, and thus they count toward a trophy for opening 300 chests.
=-=

Head to the southwest corner of the area for a scene introducing you to Aifread's Treasures, and you get '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. Henceforth, almost every new area will have two of his treasures for you to find, to a total of 61; 50 of those are needed for a trophy. You can get a '''''[[Napple]]''''' and '''''[[Wild Bird Egg]] x3''''' in the nearby residence on the northwestern side of town... Thief. Enter the Mayor's house and check the counter/dresser on the eastern side of the house (near the stairs and under a window) for '''''[[300 gald]]'''''. Head upstairs and check the bed in Room 2 for an '''''[[Apple Gel]]''''', and the nightstand in Room 1 for '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''.

Now go ahead and talk to the Mayor to rest for the night. Afterward, head to the western side of town and toward the Galia Trail to meet Elize, then hit the trail.

|* Galia Trail - East Region |

^l12|

To the southwest of where you start at the base of a tree is '''''[[900 gald]]'''''. Follow the path through the bottleneck and look at the circle of trees at the southernmost tip of the area. Check the south side of one of the trees for your first Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Bandage]]'''''. Follow the wall west as it goes north to claim a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''', then head to the northern wall and follow it for '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2'''''. Head to the '''West Region'''.

|* Galia Trail - West Region |

Follow the northern wall to a '''''[[Pudding Cake (Small)]]''''', then head to the southeast corner for a '''''[[Stun Bracelet]]'''''. From there, head north along the eastern wall and look at the second rock along the way for Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[2000 gald]]'''''. Near the end of the path is an '''''[[Orange Gel]]'''''. Continue to the next area.

+
+
+

===Kijara Seafalls===

^l13|

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                   |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries        |
|c [_] |c '' [[Meat Sauce Pasta (Small)]] '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Pet Dragon]]      '' |c [_] |c '' [[Ribbit]]             '' |
|c [_] |c '' [[700 gald]]                 '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Bronze Helm]]     '' |c [_] |c '' [[Polwigle]]           '' |
|c [_] |c '' [[Jasmine]]                  '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]]     '' |c [_] |c '' [[Crab Man]]           '' |
|c [_] |c '' [[Melange Gel]]              '' |c-3 [_] |c-3 '' [[Guardian Emblem]] '' |c [_] |c '' [[Merfish]]            '' |
|c [_] |c '' [[Heal Bangle]]              '' |c                                         [_] |c '' [[Coastal Mandragora]] '' |
|c [_] |c '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x6     '' |c                                         [_] |c '' [[Greater Demon]] (!)  '' |

''(!) = [[BOSS BATTLE #02]]''

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** After boss (Etc.): '''''[[A Monster That Size]]'''''
+

|* East Beach |

Check out the south side of the body of water for '''''[[Meat Sauce Pasta (Small)]]''''', then scale the first cliff to the southwest and head south for '''''[[700 gald]]'''''. Continue up the next cliff and follow the oval all the way around for '''''[[Jasmine]]'''''. Now drop into the western area to proceed.

|* Central Area |

Head to the southern cave for a '''''[[Melange Gel]]''''', and ignore the cliffs for now. Go through the northwestern mini-tunnel to the other side of the rock wall. Turn around; on the northern end of the rock wall is one of Aifread's Treasures, '''''[[Pet Dragon]]'''''. The only other thing in this area is a chest to the west containing a '''''[[Bronze Helm]]'''''. Be sure to equip it!

Now go back to the beginning of the area and climb the cliffs near the cave; there is a chest to the west containing '''''[[Heal Bangle]]'''''. Jump down the southeastern cliffs to reach ground level again. From the bottom, turn north to find a chest in the wall's cavity -- it has '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6'''''. Carry on to the next area... for a nice surprise.

%
====BOSS BATTLE #02====
@r|2-LU1pIinjs
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Greater Demon]]'''''                                         '''(LV. 08)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   9800 |c       271 |c       280 |c       209 |c       197 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  14000 |c       388 |c       402 |c       300 |c       282 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  21000 |c       465 |c       481 |c       359 |c       338 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  35000 |c       582 |c       603 |c       450 |c       424 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  56000 |c       777 |c       804 |c       600 |c       565 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Fire                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Water                                                     |

This boss comes attached to a tutorial about linked artes. You might as well try chaining on this boss, as he isn't particularly difficult at the beginning. His movements start slow enough that you can tell, most of the time, when to guard. He does have two attacks he'll start spamming that both hit a wide circular range; you'd better run if he starts it. He'll thrust his antennas into the ground when he activates either of them; the difference between them is that one attack follows its target (probably you), and the other is short range.

To deal some decent damage, control Milla and use her Fireball in conjunction with either Alvin's Tiger Blade to land Hell Pyre, or Jude's Soaring Vortex for Aerial Fire. (If you have Jude's Steel and Milla's Flame Ring, then that does even more damage, though it's a bit harder to get Jude to cooperate.) Link with Alvin on occasion when he's needed to break the Demon's guard, and use Jude for normal attacks when Milla's TP runs low and he's not needed for healing. Depending on the difficulty, if you don't like playing healer, it's worth it to take control of Milla, since you'll likely be healing more often than not.

One of the cute things about ailments in this game is that if your linked partner gets one, you get one too. So watch out for weak. Oh, and don't be a dummy like Drache was. Upgrade your equipment. ;)

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items'' |
|c    400  |c      800 |c [[Poison Ward]]   |

===Nia Khera, Sanctum of Maxwell===

^l14|

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                    |

=--Note...--=
Pick up ALL the Mysterious Jewels; they're for a late game sub event. Stuff you find in towns isn't necessarily junk!
=-=

Check out the piggies. They're actually rappigs. :) Secondly, don't go to Xagut Floodmeadow unless you want to die. The enemies are high enough level to hand your ass to you in one hit.

Near the exit you wind up by is a guy with a request -- [[Incoming Monster]], then go inside the nearby house (Ivar's House) and pilfer '''''[[500 gald]]'''''. The next building, Residence 3, has an '''''[[Apple Gel]]'''''. Head across the northern bridge going east to get '''''[[Temporal Wind Stone]]''''' at the altar, then take the request, [[Offerings for Milla]], from the person standing next to it. Further east, Residence 2 has a '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]''''' inside.

The second altar is just south of here, containing '''''[[Temporal Earth Stone]]'''''. Next to the item shop is an old guy you can talk to for [[The Myth of Maxwell]] sub-event. Near the exit to the east is the request, [[Something Tasty]]. You should be able to fulfill this request immediately, assuming you got the Napple in Hamil. Check inside Residence 1 for '''''[[Sandwich (Small)]]'''''. Check out the squiggly path on the south end of the map; jump down from the bridge to the rocks on the river and check the altar for '''''[[Temporal Water Stone]]'''''. Then, west of the bridge, is the final altar and '''''[[Temporal Fire Stone]]'''''.

With that in hand, off to the '''Nia Khera Spiritway''' to the west.

|* Sapstrath Seahaven |

''Sidequests galore!''
** Approach the bulletin board for some wanted posters, part of [[The Message]]. (Never knew you had it in you, Jude!)

** Approach the sailor toward the southeast end of town for an automatic scene and sub event, [[Anticipated Reunion]].
** At the southeastern corner of town is another sub event, [[The Femme Fatale]].
** Rest at the inn for a scene and the first part of [[Those Who Act in Shadow]].
** Approach the exit to be introduced to the Devil's Arms and [[The Devil's Beasts]].
** Talk to the bounty hunter near the exit for a final request, [[The Amazing Bounty Hunter]].
+

A lot to do here, huh? Anyway, once that's all done, exit to the southwest to the Sapstrath Highroad.

Make note that the first seven enemies above are right here in the Highroad; we'll be encountering them later as well, so feel free to skip them for now.

|* Sapstrath Deepwood - Northeast Region |

Be sure to find a [[Poison Stinger]] here for [[The Femme Fatale]]. Also, you may find a [[Bacura]] here. It's a strong boss type enemy worth a lot of experience, but a bit much for this point. Be careful.

Crawl through the passage get ambushed... and the cutie finally joins!

|* Elize - Starting Equipment             |
|c '''''[[Wand]]'''''                     |
|c '''''[[Green Ribbon]]'''''             |
|c '''''[[Silk Cloak]]'''''               |
|c '''''[[Normal Hairstyle (Elize)]]''''' |
|c '''''[[Normal Attire (Elize)]]'''''    |

=--Note...--=
Now that you have four active party members, you can put two of them to work. The titles along the lines of '''Jude <3 Milla''' and '''Milla <3 Elize''' require 30 minutes of linked time. So set the strategies of all characters to "Link Often", and make sure you're always linked yourself. This isn't worth anything other than a series of titles, so if you aren't a super OCD completionist, you don't have to worry about it.
=-=

Continue up the cliff for two paths. Crawl through the path to the south for '''''[[1500 gald]]''''' in a chest, then continue west to the '''North Region'''. There's a small mob as part of [[The Amazing Bounty Hunter]], so take them out, then claim the chest containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6''''' afterward.

With that diversion out of the way, head back to the fork at the '''Northeast Region''' and drop down the western path. Along the way is '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2''''' and '''''[[Poison Ward]]''''', so grab them before moving on to the '''North Region'''.

|* North Region |

Jump down for a scene. Avoid those shrooms in the future, as they damage you. Crawl through the passage on the north side and climb the cliffs for '''''[[Mabo Curry (Small)]]'''''. Climbing the western cliff from here gets you Aifread's treasure, '''''[[Black Bunny Ears]]'''''. Jumping back down the next two cliffs to the east lets you reach the place you started at. There are, again, two exits; ignore the ivy that takes you higher and continue south to the '''South Region'''.

|* South Region |

Cross the river and climb the nearby vines to the south for '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2'''''. Grab the'''''[[Verbena]]''''' in the eastern section of the area, then climb the nearby vines all the way up for '''''[[Apple Gel]] x2''''', and '''''[[Hard Coat]]'''''.

Head back to the '''North Region''', and take the path you skipped: climb up the vines, grab the '''''[[Mysterious Liquid]] x6''''' to the east, then exit west.

|* Southwest Region |

Right next to you is '''''[[Supple Ivy]] x9''''', and at the northern tip of the area is '''''[[Holy Bottle]]'''''. Grab those, then continue southeast to another portion of the '''South Region'''.

|* South Region |

Head down the path toward the Memory Ring for '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''.

Be sure to save before carrying on. With a strong boss forthcoming, it may be smart to use a food to increase your DEF (like the Yakisoba Noodles) as well. When you're ready, continue to the next area to come across a rather giant blockade.

%
====BOSS BATTLE #03====
@r|lC9CvcwKlbk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Jiao (1)]]'''''                                              '''(LV. 13)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  11900 |c       303 |c       314 |c       259 |c       256 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  17000 |c       435 |c       450 |c       372 |c       368 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  25000 |c       521 |c       539 |c       445 |c       440 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  42500 |c       653 |c       675 |c       557 |c       552 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  68000 |c       871 |c       900 |c       744 |c       736 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Wind                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Earth                                                     |

He comes with two small fry. Be sure to get rid of them quickly so the whole party is focused on the big guy. If Jiao is chasing you, by all means ignore them. He hits like a truck. He's just slow enough to guard when he brings his hammer down to blast the area around him. You'll want to keep Elize's TP up so she can heal.

Definitely control Milla in this fight, as Jude's Soaring Vortex takes too long and keeps you open for damage. Link with him though, as tossing in an extra Final Gale and / or Aerial Fire definitely helps. Do your best to hit him with Milla's wind attacks, as they may actually stagger him. His attacks get heavier as you whittle down his HP, and they tend to either stun or knock you down. He will also summon a [[Hawk]] at some point, as well as another [[Sylvan Wolf]] or two. At this point, it's best to keep Jiao's attention yourself; otherwise he'll beat up the *rest* of your party.

In the event you have access to Fairy Circle (Milla/Elize), don't cast it too close to him unless you want to get stunned after casting. Hammer Rain is pretty good, though.

===Sharilton, City of Hails and Farewells===

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** Upon Entering: '''''[[(Traces of the Toy Peddler)]]'''''
** After Lord's Manor: '''''[[(Making Friends)]]'''''
** After Rowen Joins: '''''[[The Loyal Butler]]''''', '''''[[Eye of the Beholder]]'''''
+

Scene as you enter. Remember to keep a [[Poison Stinger]] around if you donate materials to the shops. On the western wall near the shops is the [[Jet Black Feather Trading Post]] for the [[Jet Black Feathers]] sub event. Talk to the little girl by the item shop for the second part of [[Anticipated Reunion]].

Item obsessed? The NPC on the cart at the south part of the area sells '''''[[Ice Pop]]'''''. You have to use those items to get both a '''''[[Win Stick]]''''' and a '''''[[Lose Stick]]'''''.

As you enter the '''Central Plaza''' to the southwest, there's another request waiting for you by the entrance, [[The Sad Salesman]], and across from the weapon shop is the first part of [[The Runaways]]. Near the northwest exit are a group of three attached to an automatic scene and [[The Clouds of Battle Begin to Stir]]. Go to the inn to the south of them and talk to the girl near the fireplace to finish off [[Special Delivery to the Inn]].

At '''Lord's Manor Gates''' to the far south, you'll come to a scene. You'll be allowed to speak to Rowen or Jude/Milla. The western room up the stairs has a book to read, and you can get a '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]''''' by the yellow lamp behind Elize and Driselle. Try to leave after talking to everyone for a scene.

After you leave, talk to the kid to the north and east for a '''''[[Lucky Charm]]''''' and [[Travel Protection]]. Then talk to the twins on the other side of the area for [[Pretty and Pink]]. Proceed back north to the plaza to find Alvin, that tattlejerk... Rowen is awesome... and he joins.

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Milla's Friends]]''''', '''''[[When Elize Grows Up]]''''', '''''[[Nachtigal's Consolidation of Power]]'''''

Before moving on in the story, go back to the '''Sapstrath Highroad - Southwest Region''' from Sharilton, then go north and up the vines to the '''North Branch''' and climb up the cliff to the northwest to fight a mob as part of [[The Sad Salesman]].

Now warp to '''Sapstrath Deepwood - SW Entrance'''. On the wall just north the entrance is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Elixir]] x2'''''. Yep, the game is a jerk. You should have 10 of Aifread's Treasures now, to give you the title of '''Pirate Recruit'''.

Next is '''Sapstrath Seahaven'''. Talk to the guy right at the entrance to complete [[The Amazing Bounty Hunter]]. You should also earn '''Sub Event Starter''' for completing 10 sub events. Give the lady at the northern end of town a Poison Stinger to finish [[The Femme Fatale]].

At '''Aladhi Seahaven''', head south from the entrance to find a guy selling Teepos, as part of [[Anticipated Reunion]]. Near the ships is the guy you deliver the Lucky Charm to, ending [[Travel Protection]].

In '''Nia Khera''', check out the rappigs just to the west of the peddler for... uh, wait, one of them is a piggit? Bunny pink? Pig pink? ;_; Anyway, this is for [[Rappig, Rappig]]. Talk to Ivar near the northwest exit for [[Ivar the Shaman]].

In '''Hamil''', go to the shed's basement where Elize was kept for [[A Life in Shackles]]. Then head to the Eastern District for [[The People of Hamil]].

Finally, return to entrance of the '''Sharilton - Central Plaza''' to finish [[The Sad Salesman]]. That's it for odds and ends, so shop around if you like, but when you're ready, let's continue the story by exiting Sharilton to the far southwest to go to the Culmar Trail.

''(!) = [[BOSS BATTLE #04]]''

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** If you use Rowen enough: '''''[[Milla's Reward]]'''''
** After boss: '''''[[A Show of Spirit]]''''', '''''[[A Home for Elize]]'''''
+

You can find [[Peachberry Blossoms]] in the Gathering Points here for [[Pretty and Pink]].

Back outside of the cavern, check just to the south to find a short ledge / cliff with a yellow chest; hop up there and open it for a '''''[[Seal Ward]]'''''. Jump down, then head to the northwestern cliffs. After you've climbed two vines (you'll see a tree growing off the edge of the platform), go to the southeastern edge of the cliff and jump down for '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x7'''''. Go back up the vines, then up the cliff next to you. Follow the path around to the west and north to '''''[[Panacea Bottle]] x2'''''. Afterward, head to the '''South Region'''.

|* South Region |

The nearby downward path to the west leads to '''''[[Potato Salad (Small)]]'''''. Continue up the slope, and when you reach the vines leading up, drop off the edge to the west, and you'll find Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Headband]]'''''. You can see it better from the level below. Now jump down the ledge from the east side of the vines to find a '''''[[Wind Cape]]''''', then jump to the lowest level. In the eastern tip down there is '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2'''''. Climb the vines on the pillar near there to wind up right next to the first chest of the area, then go up to the top, climbing the vines we skipped over, for a '''''[[Silver Hat]]'''''. Jump down the cliffs to the west and north to reach the '''Northwest Region'''.

|* Northwest Region |

If you want to check out the entire area below for materials, jump down from the EAST side and make your way to the first chest from there. If you don't care, jump down the western vines twice to for '''''[[Lavender]]'''''. Either way, once you have the Lavender, climb back up to the level you started on, then take the western path for a '''''[[Pure White Puffball]] x5''''' one level down. Up the vines and immediately to your right will be Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Elixir]] x2'''''. Further along will be a '''''[[Fancy Ribbon]]''''', and at the top level to the south of the last chest is '''''[[3000 gald]]'''''. Once you have all that, continue east to the '''Northeast Region'''.

|* Northeast Region |

There's a boulder to the northeast you can push down to create a shortcut. You can head back to any town now if you wish; Drache did, as she got her butt handed to her just ahead... and it was 100% effective! (Seriously though; if you didn't get any Seal Wards before, now's a good time to make sure you have them for your active party. You'll definitely need them in the upcoming battle.)

Follow the path all the way around to the south side for a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''', then proceed up the vines on the center platform to the next level for a scene.

%
====BOSS BATTLE #04====
@r|AUq3-BJFuzg
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Nameless Anomaly]]'''''                                      '''(LV. 16)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  14000 |c       369 |c       387 |c       329 |c       270 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  20000 |c       529 |c       555 |c       471 |c       388 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  30000 |c       634 |c       665 |c       564 |c       465 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  50000 |c       794 |c       832 |c       706 |c       581 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  80000 |c      1059 |c      1110 |c       942 |c       776 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Earth                                                     |

Consider using Syrup Bottles; they have limited times, but prevent ailments. This guy will inflict a bunch of 'em with mist attacks -- Arteseal, Poison, and Skillseal. He also has wide range, hard hitting attacks (one stuns!), so try to keep him away from Elize if you have her out. Consider giving her (or everyone, depending on how many you have) the Seal Ward so she can keep healing and using artes, and someone else should have the Stun Bracelet on (likely Jude, so he's always dealing damage). He can cast both a bell attack (it can confuse, but this is a larger problem on higher difficulties) or a wind attack, so be sure to stay on him and consider linking to Rowen when you see it coming.

Your best bet is using Igneous Crush (Jude's Cerberus Strike / Milla's & Rowen's Rock Trine) and chaining from there if you're lucky, getting as many in as you can per set of Linked Artes. While it is weak to Earth, Rock Trine on its own will miss most of the time, making it practically useless. You can also spam Fireball (with extra Fireballs) with Rowen from a distance, if you're having trouble.

If you have access to Recovery Heal (Jude's Recovery Ring / Elize's Recover), that would be quite lovely to use this battle, as it acts like a massive Syrup Bottle AND Panacea Bottle. Pixie Heal (Jude's Healer / Elize's Pixie Heal) also works quite nicely for mass HP recovery.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items''                |
|c     600 |c     1000 |c [[Winged Boots]], [[Earth Cape]] |

Those boots you got increase your running speed. There are two chests to the northeast and east, before you head out. They contain '''''[[Melange Gel]] x3''''' and '''''[[5000 gald]]'''''. Now warp to Sharilton.

+

The skit above is a hint to the next place you should be heading. Stop by the two twins for the next part of [[Pretty and Pink]], if you have the Peachberry Blossom they asked for. Of course, this sidequest isn't over. Continue to the ''Central Plaza'' and head straight north for a view of the windmill, then talk to the man here to start [[The Shape of Our World]], where you'll obtain the '''''[[Spirit Clime Examination Arte]]'''''.

Teleport to the '''Bermia Gorge'''. Head inside the cavern directly in front of you for [[Mystery of the Gorge]], then head back out and climb to the tip-top of the dungeon for the [[The Shape of Our World]] sub-event. Afterward, return to the client in '''Sharilton'''.

You can now traverse the entirety of '''Sapstrath Highroad - Northeast Region'''. On the wall near the southwest exit is a hole leading to '''''[[2000 gald]]'''''. Near a tree by the east of there is a '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''. Climb up the north cliff; the boulder toward the west end of the wall has Aifread's Treasure on the other side, '''''[[Black Dog Ears]]''''', and there is also a chest up here containing '''''[[Hard Scale]] x7'''''.

If you're on Milla's path, see [[Talys Highroad (Jude)]] right now. It's an optional area for Milla, and the levels can be helpful.

With that diversion out of the way, go ahead and rest at the Lord's Manor, then send Rowen.

* As Milla, you'll be forced north to go shopping... then a battle that you can't win. You'll automatically get '''''[[Milla's Pendant]]'''''. For her next section, click [[Fort Gandala (Milla)]].
* As Jude, you'll have to run to the Central Plaza, then to the Manor. Afterward, before leaving to Talys Highroad, go to the Central Plaza to and look for a group of two people to see [[Military Secrets]].

You may find a Bacura here. Probably still a bad time to attempt fighting it.

Just north of the entrance is a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''', and continue following the eastern wall as it goes north, then west. Keep an eye out for a hole; crawl through it for an '''''[[Hourglass]]'''''. Head for the southern cliff, now; behind a rock along the wall is Aifread's Treasure,  '''''[[Sly Glasses]]'''''. Further west along the wall is a cavity to crawl in for '''''[[3000 gald]]'''''. Once you have that, hop back down and take the northwestern exit.

|* West Region |

Climb the central cliff for '''''[[Fine Down]] x8'''''. To the northeast of it, below the east cliff, is '''''[[Tofu Cracker (Small)]]'''''. Head up the eastern cliff and make your way to the northern wall for a hole hiding an '''''[[All-Divide]]'''''. Now, don't go to the Fort just yet; climb up the cliff to the southwest to the... southwest branch.

|* Southwest Branch |

By the pillar's east side is '''''[[Rosemary]]'''''. On the wall by the southeast corner, near a cactus, is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. In the wall a little southeast of there is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x7'''''. Finally, just on the southwest side of the pond here are a couple of trees with a chest between them; it has '''''[[Broken Fang]] x10'''''. With that done, return to the West Region and continue west to Fort Gandala.

===Fort Gandala (Jude)===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                          |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Elevator Key]]         '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Silver Helm]]            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Rashugal Spiritcorps Channeler]] '' |

|c   [_] |c   '' [[Holy Bottle]] x2       '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fine Boots]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Rashugal Battlecorps Soldier]]   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[French Toast (Small)]] '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Splint Mail]]            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Bladed Boar]]                    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5 '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[5000 gald]]              '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Golem]]                          '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[All-Divide]]           '' |c-2 [_] |c-2 '' [[Blue Chamomile]]         '' |c-2 [_] |c-2 '' [[Golem Shade]]                    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]] x2       '' |

=--Note...--=
If you miss a particular enemy, you can come back at the end of the game and get it.
=-=

You'll automatically receive the '''''[[Elevator Key]]''''' after the scene. Also, make note that a lot of exits are blocked at the moment, but will appear on the map.

Right next to where you start is '''''[[Melange Gel]] x2'''''. Head all the way to the other side of the area; in front of the southwest statue is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. Behind one of the carriages is '''''[[Holy Bottle]] x2'''''. Take the north door from here. On the northern railing, all the way to the west, is '''''[[French Toast (Small)]]''''', then take the elevator to B1. Grab the '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''''' along the wall to the northeast, then head in the room for an '''''[[All-Divide]]'''''.

On 3F, grab '''''[[Life Bottle]] x2''''' next to the east exit, and the '''''[[Silver Helm]]''''' on the northwest end of the area. Enter the west room and push the block to make a path up. At the bottom, take the northwest lift to find another block. Move it below for '''''[[1500 gald]]''''' and '''''[[Pure White Puffball]] x5''''' Crawl in the hole by the treasures and make your way to the lift in there, then crawl through the hole on the second floor for a fight and the '''''[[Control Room Key]]'''''. Go ahead and unlock the door, but you need to crawl back through the hole.

Take the block down the lift and make a path to '''''[[Fine Boots]]''''', then push it to the north end of the room to make a path to the second hole. In there, make a path to the '''''[[Splint Mail]]''''', then push the block to the southeast wall to get '''''[[5000 gald]]'''''. On 2F, grab the '''''[[Blue Chamomile]]''''' by the west exit. Exit through the westernmost door on 1F to get to the carriages, and go straight ahead to the next door to find your destination... and a fight against mooks. There's only one way to go, and you get to see the results of Milla's insanity.

===Fort Gandala (Milla)===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                          |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |

And Elize is deadweight. Lovely. Check the sink in the cell for '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2'''''. At the southern end of the next room is '''''[[Sandwich (Medium)]]'''''. Head into '''Warehouse 02''' for a fight and '''''[[Control Room Key]]'''''. Go up to 3F from that room, grab the box, push it to the lift, then make a way up to the chest below. You get '''''[[Gold Dust]] x10'''''. Crawl through the hole, then take the next lift at the far end of the room. There's another hole to crawl through up there, amidst the boxes, for '''''[[2500 gald]]''''' and '''''[[Cat Hairband]]'''''. Back to the pushable box; down the lift and claim your '''''[[Melange Gel]] x2'''''. Back through the hole, head up the lift and leave the room.

Outside, across the small bridge is '''''[[Holy Bottle]] x2'''''. Consider using them if the enemies have roughed you up too much. Enter '''Warehouse 04''' for another encounter. You get '''''[[Elevator Key]]''''' In this room, there is a box you can push out of the way for '''''[[Gold Dust]] x10'''''. Leave the room, and head for the elevator in the middle of the area.

At '''B1''', there is a chest containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''''', then head in the door. Pull the box on the lift, go up, and push it to the north to get '''''[[Fine Boots]]''''', then push it to get up the south cliff for '''''[[Pure White Puffball]] x5'''''. Push the box up there on top of your other one, and drag 'em both down the lift, then make a path to the '''''[[Long Coat]]''''' and '''''[[5000 gald]]'''''. Take the lift up, and leave. Right next to the door is '''''[[Lemon Gel]] x2'''''. Go into the final room for one  hell of a scene.

Milla is crazy.

===Sharilton Again===

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Jude's Hometown]]''''', '''''[[Different Paths]]''''', '''''[[Ilbert the Conductor]]'''''
+

Before Milla wakes up, head to the inn to find Alvin, then back to the Manor.

Once Sleeping Beauty does wake up...

Turn right around and go to the Lord's Manor. Talk to Elize for [[Teepo: Back in Action]]. Enter the west room and talk to Driselle for [[Cline and Driselle]]. Buy any healing items you need now.

Now take the ''Sapstrath Highroad'' to ''Sapstrath Seahaven''. You'll encounter scenes along the way, and if you're on Jude's side, you'll get '''''[[Milla's Pendant]]'''''. There's also a fight with a boar; if you're used to Milla, be sure to practice against it and some of the other enemies around. Continue to the Seahaven...

%
====BOSS BATTLE #05====
@r|mpAre9KXTDw
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Ivar (1)]]'''''                                              '''(LV. 17)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   4900 |c       412 |c       415 |c       333 |c       341 |
|c ''Normal''             |c   7000 |c       590 |c       595 |c       477 |c       488 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  10500 |c       707 |c       713 |c       572 |c       585 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  17500 |c       885 |c       892 |c       716 |c       732 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  28000 |c      1180 |c      1190 |c       955 |c       976 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Earth                                                     |

If you're used to Milla (Drache was!), this is really awkward, but can be done. Aqua Sweep will knock him down and give you time to recover, just make sure to run away from him first. His combos are pretty damaging, and the main problem to anyone not used to Jude is healing. Don't use Healer; Ivar's too fast for that. He'll also Seal your artes, get behind you, and break your guard. Seal Ward isn't a bad item! Keep dodging his combos, and try to free run and bait him into attacking air. He will attack faster than you; don't try to out speed him. Demon Fist can be used from a distance, but don't overdo it.

Jude's Snap Pivot, activated by backstepping away from an enemy's attack, is actually quite a nice ability as it gets him behind the enemy. It makes things a looooot easier. If you don't have it mastered, the battle is simple enough that it can be done without, but it will be harder.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Drop''     |
|c     700 |c     1000 |c [[Lavender]] |

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                        |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |

If the enemies kick your butt, you can try to avoid them or come back later. They're kind of tough, at least with two party members.

Climb up the cliff and search the wall for a cavity containing '''''[[Thief's Cape]]'''''. Down the north side of the cliff; on a tree is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Half-frame Glasses]]'''''. Between a few trees before the path turns north, there is a chest containing '''''[[Herb]] x10'''''. On a tree just to the east of it is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. Continue along till you hit a cliff; on the eastern edge of it is a chest containing '''''[[Blue Saffron]]'''''. Finally, by the body of water is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Don't explore the mine you wind up next to unless you want to die... but go ahead and enter through that small hole to create a world map shortcut. Go to '''Felgana Mine''', as you're supposed to.

===Felgana Mine===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                    |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Lemon Gel]]           '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fossilized Shell]] x10'' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Bat]]                         '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Do-Gooder Jude]]'''''
+

* Materials in Rocks
** Block of Quartz
** Mud Rock
** Rock Salt
** Ancient Fossilized Insect

The rocks you can mine here may yield a Block of Quartz, so be sure to get one for [[Heavy Metal Collector]]. Just mine every rock you see; they don't always appear, except the ones covering holes.

The path immediately to the north of the exit has a '''''[[Lemon Gel]]''''' at the end. Carry along for a scene... and the ability to break rocks. There's only one point to mine at: the southern part of the room, near the end of the path. The next room has a thousand tiny paths to take, as well as rocks to mine.

|* Natural Tunnel |

Head west; along the way is a rock to break which may have a Loot Bag inside the hole it's covering (there are plenty of rocks like this). The nearby chest at the end of the path has an '''''[[Orange Gel]]'''''.

Now head for the eastern path to the south. Mine the first rock, just south of the entrance, and crawl in the hole for '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x4'''''. At the bottom of the path is a '''''[[Soba Omelette (Small)]]'''''. Take the path southwest for an earthquake, then mine the north and south walls to create paths, and head through the south one. The next rock you come to may lead to a Loot Bag, and the one in the passage near it leads to '''''[[Melange Gel]] x3'''''.

At the fork, go northeast and one of the rocks in the passage, which leads to '''''[[Gold Dust]] x7'''''. Return to the fork and take the north route. One of the rocks in the passage leads to an '''''[[Earth Cape]]'''''. Near the cliff's edge is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Backpack]]'''''.

|* Shaft 4 |

Mine your way west, take the northeast path at the fork, then south at the main shaft to a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''' and a rock to break, leading to '''''[[Blue Jasmine]]'''''. North of that area, on the west wall, is a rock covering a hole (with a Loot Bag inside, if anything) across from it. At the north tip of the area is '''''[[Fossilized Shell]] x10''''', and, immediately to the west of it is an Aifread's Treasure containing '''''[[5000 gald]]'''''.

Before continuing to the west, take the south path for '''''[[Insect Wings]] x6''''', and a rock covering a hole. Further along the path is a second rock that leads to '''''[[Savory]]'''''. Back to the main path, head straight west to bump into '''''[[Hard Hat]]'''''. On the wall opposite the chest is a rock covering a hole. All the way south is '''''[[Apple Gel]] x3''''', a rock covering the way to '''''[[Sage]]''''', as well as another rock over a hole.

Break the east wall, but head northwest at the fork. Break the rock through there to claim '''''[[2500 gald]]''''' on the other side. Break the wall, if you want, and proceed to the Memory Ring and next room, '''Monster Nest'''. You know where this is going.

%
====BOSS BATTLE #06====
@r|XNlIhgsfR60
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Hammerzamm (1)]]'''''                                        '''(LV. 22)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   6300 |c       518 |c       445 |c       409 |c       419 |
|c ''Normal''             |c   9000 |c       740 |c       636 |c       586 |c       600 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  13500 |c       888 |c       763 |c       702 |c       719 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  22500 |c      1111 |c       955 |c       879 |c       900 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  36000 |c      1481 |c      1273 |c      1172 |c      1201 |

This one has a spray attack and burrows underground to attack, but isn't particularly fast or hard hitting. However, when you get his HP down to a certain point, he does have a fairly fast underground attack that keeps following you; backstep from it. Jude has a variety of good linked artes with Leia, but Pixie Heal is particularly useful. Annoyingly, this guy will summon Worm Shades. Don't divert your attention to them; big guy will cause you more problems than a spell every so often. On higher difficulties, Arteseal is an annoyance.

It would not be a bad idea to knock him down (and again in the next battle!) for that stealable item.

|c ''EXP''    |c ''Gald''    |c ''Dropped Items''                  |c ''Stealable Items'' |
|c        800 |c        1200 |c [[Heavy Treat]], [[Specific Plus]] |c [[Seal Ward]]       |

But wait, there's more!

|*+6 '''''[[Hammerzamm (2)]]'''''                                        '''(LV. 22)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  15400 |c       647 |c       556 |c       512 |c       524 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  22000 |c       926 |c       795 |c       733 |c       751 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  33000 |c      1110 |c       954 |c       879 |c       900 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  55000 |c      1389 |c      1193 |c      1099 |c      1127 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  88000 |c      1852 |c      1501 |c      1466 |c      1502 |

Those items he just dropped should come in handy.

He hits harder this time, and has more than double the HP. Not to mention he inflicts Arteseal! Have someone equip Seal Charm, and everyone else can have a Seal Ward. Don't link with Leia except for stealing and the very occasional linked arte; she'll back off and heal if she isn't attached to you, and the battle will go more smoothly. The major thing to watch out for is that he sometimes lunges forward, instead of up, when underground. He also likes to stun a lot and even grab you like the smaller worms. Toward the end, he'll get ridiculously fast with going underground, then he'll start causing rocks to fall. And yes, he'll summon a worm again.

==Chapter 2==

===Leronde===

First of all, go back to the guy in the inn to complete [[Heavy Metal Collector]], then go to the '''Mathis Clinic''', then the Seahaven. After that, go into the '''Mathis Clinic - Archives''' for a hilarious sub event, [[Milla and Books]]. Right next to the entrance of the clinic, talk to Ellen to rest, and head to the inn for the next scene. Talk to Sonia at the inn afterward for [[Leia's Disappearance]]. Now go on to the Seahaven and, after the scene, get '''''[[Leia's Notes]]'''''.

Note that everyone that rejoined has new equipment -- [[Air Rod]], [[Striped Ribbon]], [[Silver Cloak]], [[Tourbillon]], [[Hunting Beret]], [[Silver Coat]], [[Stormbringer]], [[Hard Hat]], and [[Battle Suit]].

|* Lakutam Seahaven |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Leia the Stowaway]]''''', '''''[[(Getting it Over With)]]''''', '''''[[In Good Hands]]''''', '''''[[Leia's Notes (Skit)]]'''''
** On Lakutam Highroad: '''''[[(Childhood Memories)]]''''', '''''[[(The Sea at Sunset)]]''''', '''''[[The Aspyrixis]]'''''
+

=--Note...--=
Listen to every word in this section or die.

...Or miss a couple skits. You can buy them in the grade shop if you miss 'em.
=-=

Attempt to leave town for a scene. Now leave, and get all the skits you see listed (mainly the first two, but you might as well get the third). You will not see them otherwise.

Return to the Seahaven.

Go to the bulletin board for the final part of [[The Message]], then go north toward the downward stairs to automatically trigger [[Milla's Pendant (Event)]]. Continue north from there for [[The Edge of the World]] to appear, then talk to the man nearby for [[The Topknot Master]]. On the opposite side of the area, talk to the two ladies for the first part of [[Sisterhood]]. Finally, talk to the guy across from the accessory shop for [[Buried Treasure]] and a '''''[[Rare Vase]]'''''.

Might as well take care of [[Buried Treasure]] now; the shop you want is facing the Highroad exit. While in Sharilton, head to the '''Central Plaza''' and talk to the lady near the south exit for [[Orange Soup]]. Food Vendor must be level 5 or higher to buy one, so it should be easy. Approach the east mansion at '''Lord's Manor Gates''' for [[Rowen's Honor]].

=--Note...--=
You get to pick between a sub event and a skit. Either do Alvin and Derrick, or get a skit later on. Why? Dunno, but as far as Drache can tell, that's the condition for the skit to appear. Again, you can always buy skits in the grade shop later.

Also, don't enter Leronde's Inn. You'll miss another skit if you do that sidequest too early.
=-=

Back to '''Leronde''', near the Voltea Woods Entrance. Talk to the guy right by the exit for [[The Elder's Plea]] and '''''[[Ex-Miner's Wine]]'''''.

Back inside the inn, and talk to Warrick for [[Beat the Bandits]] (this request is probably too much for you, at the moment), then to the Clinic for [[Alvin and Derrick]]. Go ahead and deliver the Wine to Felgana Mine's deepest part (southern tip of that room) and return to finish the request.

Be sure that your equipment is top notch before proceeding. If you're anything like Drache (stingy), then it's been a couple bosses since you bothered upgrading.

In a hole in the wall just north of there is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Carry on to the '''Northeast Region'''. Note that a Memory Ring is thrown in front of you.

====BOSS BATTLE #07====
@r|2_aeQiKIY8s
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Brutaur]]'''''                                               '''(LV. 24)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |

Be careful to not get trapped against the edge, or in front of his charge; if you aren't guarding, you'll probably die. One of the more annoying things he does is summon the local monsters to assist him. If you have subpar equipment, he's absolutely going to kill you. Even with the best you can get, he hits incredibly hard, so block or die. There's no fast or easy way; bring a lot of items. He's also capable of stunning and inflicting Linkseal, as well as digging underground to attack you (backstep away from that one). As he dies, he'll rampage around and call a bunch of enemies. Obnoxious, but can be dealt with.

===Xian Du===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |*+4 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Dark Bottle]]         '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Insurgent Soldier]]           '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Harpy]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Holy Bottle]]         '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Sylvan Crab]]                 '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Spyrix Warrior 1]] (!)        '' |
|c-3 [_] |c-3 '' [[Syrup Bottle]]        '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Insurgent Lead Striker]]      '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Spyrix Warrior 2]] (!)        '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Close Call]]''''', '''''[[(Those Xian Du Statues)]]''''', '''''[[The Spa Retreat Package]]'''''
** After finding Wyverns: '''''[[Favorite Pets]]'''''
** After Coliseum: '''''[[The Coliseum]]''''', '''''[[Runaway Teen]]'''''
** After Boss: '''''[[Levels of Spyrix]]''''', '''''[[Too Close for Comfort]]''''' (depends on linked time with Jude/Leia, probably, and you have to run out of food... you can get this later, don't worry)

You'll be stuck in a series of scenes. Poke around in the inn's rooms for a '''''[[Dark Bottle]]''''', a '''''[[Holy Bottle]]''''', and a '''''[[Syrup Bottle]]'''''. The shops are up the elevator if you need 'em. Just above the boat leading to the Xagut Floodmeadow (you'll have to talk to someone if you want to go there) is [[The Wandering Youth]].

To find a scene about Wyverns, take the northeast elevator. It's east of the central bridge and up the north stairs. Next to the statue by the west exit is the first part of '''''[[The History of Auj Oule]]'''''. Head up the elevator at the northwest section of the area for the beginning of [[The Cause of Shifting Spirit Climes]]. Then take the boat at the north end of the area to reach the '''Coliseum'''. Talk to Yurgen twice for a fight, then sleep at the inn to have the party split in half.

As Milla, go back to the place where the rock fell. As Jude, head to the east side of the bridge. Afterward, head to the Coliseum and enter the tournament. It'll be easy to get through the first three battles. And then plot happens, and people separate again.

For Milla, go across the bridge and take the south stairs up to bump into a scene, then cross the bridge again for another. For Jude, head north from the inn to bump into a scene, then cross the bridge. At the Coliseum... a fun scene and boss. You won't have access to Alvin or Elize for this fight.

===Royal Hunting Grounds===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                    |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |

In the Gathering Points here, be sure to get a Peach Elephant Tusk for [[Pretty and Pink]].

From the entrance, go northwest and climb up one level. Along the wall is a hole leading to '''''[[Lavender]]'''''. Follow the wall to the next platform to climb up and a '''''[[Mind Ward]]'''''. Head south to the opposite wall's elevated region for a hole containing '''''[[Hazardous Liquid]] x5'''''. Follow the wall east and look in the second set of trees you see for Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Topknot]]'''''. This is related to [[The Topknot Master]]. Drop down the cliff and hug the east wall till you find a hole containing '''''[[Specific]]'''''.

|* Central Region |

In the corner to the north of the entrance is a '''''[[Beef Bowl (Small)]]'''''. Continue following that wall to come to a cliff. Up there is a hole leading to '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6'''''. The rock in front of the hole has Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]''''' on it. Just to the north of the cliff on the opposite wall is '''''[[Panacea Bottle]] x2'''''. Along the easternmost cliff's wall is a hole leading to '''''[[3000 gald]]'''''.

|* North Region |

By a tree to the north of the entrance is '''''[[Fur]] x8'''''. Climb the nearby cliff to fight the bandits for [[Punish the Poachers]]. Then claim the '''''[[Melange Gel]]''''' behind them. At the top of the southern cliff is a cavity containing '''''[[Treat]]'''''. Up the northern cliff is another cavity which has '''''[[Blue Savory]]'''''. In the east wall, close to the boulders by the central cliff, is a hole in the wall leading to '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. That's all for this area.

===Labari Hollow===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                          |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c  ''[[Tofu Miso Soup (Small)]]''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Blue Basil]]          ''     |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Mine Plant]]                  '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** After losing Elize again: '''''[[Alvin's Wound]]''''', '''''[[The Mercenary-Client Privilege]]'''''
** After getting her back: '''''[[Elize's Stalker]]'''''
+

You may find a Bronze Bacura here. It's a boss type, but weaker than your average story boss. Make sure to have your healer set to Prioritize Healing. They also appear in a future area, so don't feel like you have to fight it immediately... though you should be able to handle it.

This place is a four layered mess. Head into '''Sector 9''' to the west for '''''[[Tofu Miso Soup (Small)]]'''''. Outside, head all the way north for '''''[[Giant Shell]] x7'''''. Head around to the south side, and follow the path all the way to a '''''[[Stone Ward]]'''''. Cross the bridge to come to a '''''[[Battle Guard]]'''''. Enter '''Sector 7''', then exit to the other side.

Jump down to the second layer and enter '''Sector 4''' for a '''''[[Treat]]'''''. Now enter the neighboring '''Sector 3'''; go to the northeast room for a '''''[[Life Bottle]]''''', then exit to the southwest. Take the outside path all the way south to get '''''[[Melange Gel]]'''''. Cross the bridge, but stop where the first one passes above it. On the higher bridge is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Goofy Glasses]]'''''. Carry on to the east for a '''''[[Syrup Bottle]]'''''. Enter '''Sector 5''' for '''''[[Blue Basil]]''''', then go to '''Sector 6'''. The second south path has '''''[[2000 gald]]'''''... and the rest of your party!

|* After Reuniting |

Exit south, and hop down to the third layer. Enter '''Sector 1''' to the west, but before leaving, right next to the other exit is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Skill Tome: "Gifted Healer"]]'''''. Outside is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Back to the other side of Sector 1, and follow the circle till it branches northeast for '''''[[Crown Feather]] x10''''', then enter '''Sector 2''' for '''''[[Verbena]] x5'''''. Outside, the bottom layer has '''''[[Middy Blouse]]''''' and '''''[[3000 gald]]'''''. Now start the trek outta here. No world map warping, which mean you'll come to a scene... poor Elize. Carry along the bridge to get Elize back.

|* Xian Du |
+
|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Mysterious Jewel]]    '' |


*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Gambling Troubles]]''''', '''''[[(Alvin's Acquaintance)]]''''', '''''[[(Introductions in Xian Du)]]''''', '''''[[(A Hotel for the Night)]]'''''
** After finding Yurgen: '''''[[Exodus' Shadow]]''''', '''''[[(Nostalgia for Nia Khera)]]'''''
+

There's going to be a lot of subquesting, going by all the skits around. Finish off [[Punish the Poachers]] by talking to the person by the Hunting Grounds exit. To fiiiiinally meet Alvin's mother for the first part of [[Mother and Child]], head up the south stairs, take the elevator, and enter the residence. Afterward, talk to her again to complete the event. Poke around the house for a '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''.

Cross the bridge to come to a scene. Then head for the hotel to start [[The Aftermath]]. Also in the inn is Karla, who you can speak to for the second part of [[The History of Auj Oule]]. Head for the coliseum and talk to the guy up the stairs for [[Potent Potions of the Kitarl Clan]], and go ahead and give him what he wants (if you don't have one, you can go to Xagut Floodmeadow or Labari Hollow). You can fight at the coliseum, now.

Plot? What plot? Time to do some optional areas. Take the boat to Xagut Floodmeadow. And yes, there will be more sidequesting after that.

===Xagut Floodmeadow===

^l23|

^l24|

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                    |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Basil]]               '' |c   [_] |c   ''[[Great Tree's Fruit]] x2'' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Bog Chirpee]]                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[10000 gald]]          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[5000 gald]]           '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Plated Boar]]                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Verbena]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Savory]]              '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Water Djinn]]                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Mysterious Jewel]]    '' |c   [_] |c   ''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10'' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Cockatrice]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jasmine]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Saffron]]             '' |c-2 [_] |c-2 ''     [[Gentleman]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Omega Elixir]]        '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Chamomile]]           '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Teepo and the Four Great Spirits]]''''', '''''[[Ambidexterity]]''''', '''''[[Book Smart Jude]]'''''
+

The enemies here are somewhat strong for you, but manageable. Be very careful around Gentlemen; they're quite strong, but give good EXP. Follow the south wall; by a tree roughly southeast of the boat is '''''[[Basil]]'''''. Directly east of there, on a tree near the east wall, is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[10000 gald]]'''''. Just southwest of there, by a rock, is '''''[[Verbena]]'''''. At the southern tip of the area is a hole leading to '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. Near the exit is the guy you need to speak with to finish [[The Wandering Youth]].

|* Northeast Region |

Look between the trees to the west for '''''[[Jasmine]]'''''. Drop down to the second layer and head all the way to the eastern tip of the area for '''''[[Omega Elixir]]'''''. Down to the next layer; near the west wall is '''''[[Great Tree's Fruit]] x2'''''. Take the southeast exit.

=--Note...--=
Take the southwest exit if you really want, but ''DO NOT FIGHT THE CAT''. It's a Devil's Beast and will absolutely curbstomp you.
=-=

|* Southeast Region |

Follow the west wall to find a hole leading to '''''[[5000 gald]]''''', then follow the opposite wall south to find '''''[[Savory]]''''' near a rock by the wall. Jump down the cliff; right below it is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10'''''. Not-so-hidden on the north wall is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Black Dog's Muzzle]]'''''. Continue following that wall to come to '''''[[Saffron]]'''''.

|* South Region |

Head to the eastern tip of the area to find '''''[[Chamomile]]''''', and west from there, about in the middle of the area, is '''''[[Lavender]]'''''.

|* Odds and Ends |

Head toward the rappigs for a scene with the people who gave Milla her glass bead... For Milla, there's an easy fight, and for Jude, there's a separate scene with Ivar. This completes [[Milla's Pendant]].

Now head to '''Sharilton''' and give the pink obsessed twins their Peach Elephant Tusk for the second part of [[Pretty and Pink]].

At '''Lakutam Seahaven''', return to the Topknot Master to finish [[The Topknot Master]]. Moe. Head to the inn for [[Spirit Clime Trouble]]. This won't be any trouble; head to the pond at '''Lakutam Highroad - Central Region''' and take 'em out.

Finally, head to the bottom of '''Labari Hollow''' for [[Infiltrate the Research Center]]. Yes, Tales, you are a butthole series when it comes to sidequests. And Drache is the sort to hold grudges; she still remembers her third playthrough for a certain spear for a certain Krityan.
