===Old Vicalle Mine===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10'' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Gentlegnome]]                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Rage Glasses]]        '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Salamander]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Specific Plus]]       '' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Insurgent Striker]] (SE)      '' |
|c   [_] |c  ''[[Skill Tome: "Pinprick"]]'' |c   [_] |c   ''     [[Tree Crab]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Jasmine]]         '' |c-4 [_] |c-4 ''     [[Dusk Goblin]]                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Echore]]              '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Mysterious Jewel]]    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Dragon Ash]] x3       '' |

If you don't have this place unlocked, go so Voltea Woods - Northeast Branch and crawl in the hole to the northeast.

First of all, watch out for the Gentlegnomes. They're about as strong as Gentlemen, but at least have a weakness to exploit... and they're good for EXP, particularly with food. If you ever want to grind, these guys are a good choice.

=--Note...--=
Another Devil's Beast is coming up. AVOID.
=-=

Head east for '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10'''''. Right as the path turns, along the east wall, is a SNEAKY hole leading to '''''[[Dragon Ash]] x3'''''. Now head into the west room. The pillar to the north has Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Rage Glasses]]'''''. Beat up the bandits for [[Beat the Bandits]], then jump down to the lower southern area (and be sure to avoid that Beast). At the western end is '''''[[Specific Plus]]'''''.

Go to the '''North Region''' of the mine. Go into the west area and check behind the second rock there for Aifread's treasure, '''''[[Skill Tome: "Pinprick"]]''''', and in the wall southwest of there is a hole containing '''''[[Echore]]'''''. Don't equip the Tome's skill unless you want to try for huge combos. Now take the north path; at the west end is '''''[[Red Jasmine]]''''', and at on the east end, along the south wall, is a hole you can crawl into for '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. That's it for here.

|* Leronde |

Talk to Warrick at the Lodge to complete [[Beat the Bandits]].

Now on to the main event: Xian Du's west exit is where you want to go.

Right next to the entrance is '''''[[Elixir]]''''', and the northeast end of the area has '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. From there, hug the wall and follow it south; the boulder you bump into has Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Skill Tome: "Joyful Gains"]]''''', on it. Continue following the wall to come to a hole containing '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]'''''. Go all the way back to the Central Region, then take the northwest exit.

|* Northwest Region |

Follow the wall north for a '''''[[Pot au Feu (Small)]]''''' in a hole. On the opposite wall, go east from the entrance for a '''''[[Treat]]''''', and further east for a cavity with '''''[[Orange Gel]] x3''''' inside. East of the exit to Kanbalar, by a tree, is '''''[[Pineapple Gel]]'''''.

====BOSS BATTLE #09====

|*+6 '''''[[Presa (1)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 30)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  15400 |c       758 |c       712 |c      1065 |c       910 |

|c ''Hard''               |c  55000 |c      1740 |c      1643 |c      2341 |c      1951 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  88000 |c      2354 |c      2224 |c      3139 |c      2602 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Fire                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Water                                                     |

Presa is capable of throwing stuff at you (it stuns!) and casting artes. Stay on her; the AI cannot be relied upon to prevent her from casting artes, so they're better off occupying Wingul. Avoid getting close to both of them; one will shred you while the other will use that time to cast artes. It's impossible to leave the trap once in it. Separate, they're easy. Together, you're probably dead. And they will come together, like your own AI allies do, to protect each other, so you're just going to have to find a way to survive during those moments.

On higher difficulties, they may confuse you. Definitely the most obnoxious of ailments. Wingul also tends to like casting Arrivederci and Flame Ring. His spells are much less deadly than Presa's; they're more of an annoyance.

===Back in Xian Du===

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[(The Oddly Popular Karla)]]''''', '''''[[(Let's Test it Back at the Hotel)]]''''', '''''[[(Come on, It's Time for Bed)]]''''', '''''[[(Whither Hamil)]]''''', '''''[[Wingul's Words]]'''''
** After meeting Karla: '''''[[(A Question for Karla)]]'''''

Near the stairs leading to the Xagut Floodmeadow boat is a person you can talk to for the first part of [[Poetry and Dictionaries]]. Head toward the inn for a scene, the second part of [[Those Who Act in Shadow]], then rest at the inn, now that you have a [[Heart Herb]], for [[The Aftermath]]. '''Hic'''. On the second floor of the inn is Karla, for the third part of [[The History of Auj Oule]]. For the fourth part, head to the Coliseum and go up the stairs to talk to Karla once again.

Now, to '''Hamil''' for [[Reawakened Memories]]. Before moving on, enter the residence for [[Find the Villagers]]. To complete these events, go to '''Aladhi Seahaven''' for an automatic scene, then to '''Xian Du's''' bridge. Return to '''Hamil''' to meet the new residents for [[It Does a Body Good]]. Head to the Mathis Clinic for [[Jude's Substitute]]. To '''Hamil''' once again to complete the event... and see the change!

At '''Xian Du''', finish [[Reawakened Memories]] by heading for the bridge. Time to move on with the plot; talk to Yurgen by the wyverns... and a boss that might be familiar to anyone that played Vesperia.

====BOSS BATTLE #10====
@r|UhMnjtwKnIc
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Pterobronc]]'''''                                            '''(LV. 32)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  25200 |c      1135 |c       762 |c      1131 |c       720 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  36000 |c      1622 |c      1218 |c      1616 |c      1159 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  54000 |c      1946 |c      1521 |c      1938 |c      1450 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  90000 |c      2434 |c      1978 |c      2424 |c      1888 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 144000 |c      3245 |c      2737 |c      3233 |c      2618 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Wind                                                      |

A very mobile boss; hard to keep hitting. Obnoxiously, it spins to attack a very wide range which can keep staggering you, over and over. It's possible to get inside the attack radius so he can't hit you, though. It can also inflict you with Curse with its beam of darkness attack, along with Paralysis from another attack. Elize's Dispel is invaluable (if you don't have it, use the Jude/Elize Recover Heal). Since it's weak to water, Rowen isn't a bad choice for his Splash and Blue Sphere, as well as for Spash Beam (Rowen/Jude). Later in the fight, it starts to use fireballs and whirlwinds.

Overall, not a difficult boss. Just hard to keep in one place except with knockdown attacks.

===Fennmont Again===

|*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                      |

* In the inn's rooms: '''''[[Apple Gel]]''''' and '''''[[100 gald]]'''''

%
====BOSS BATTLE #11====
@r|CCRJG_kwbcA
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Agria (1)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 33)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  21000 |c       702 |c       597 |c       591 |c       556 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  30000 |c      1176 |c      1026 |c      1102 |c      1010 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  45000 |c      1491 |c      1310 |c      1442 |c      1312 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  75000 |c      1964 |c      1738 |c      1953 |c      1765 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 120000 |c      2752 |c      2452 |c      2804 |c      2520 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Fire                                                      |

Strangely low stats, for a boss, and she has an odd obsession with using Lemon Gels (steal it to make her stop).

But! She'll throw the first Mystic Arte of the game on you, which will harm the entire party (maybe even kill someone, if you're unlucky). Don't be afraid to use a Treat after it... and bring out Elize, if you haven't, so she can Dispel and protect against Burn. If you see her overlimit, run. Your linked partner will follow you, at least, and she'll hopefully chase you through her entire overlimit instead of unleashing a Mystic Arte. The reason for this is because, to unleash a Mystic Arte, an Arcane Arte must connect with its target first. This applies to both you and the enemy.

As she dies, she'll spam a fire attack that hits a small area around her; it's hard to get a hit in if you stay too close to her. Mystic Arte aside, she's generally a pushover.

Naturally, you can just bust your way into the palace. No problem. On 2F, fight your way to the next room. Enter the southwest door, Guard Garrison 1, for an '''''[[Earth Cap]]'''''. Check around the Conference Room for '''''[[Geode]] x7''''', '''''[[Red Sage]]''''', and, in a chest, '''''[[Dark Cape]]'''''. Check Guard Garrison 2 for '''''[[Sharp Pincers]] x6''''', a '''''[[Holy Bottle]]''''', and a chest containing '''''[[Fruit n' Cheese (Small)]]'''''. Exit to the Entrance Hall through the northeast door, and turn around to find Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Party Hat]]''''', then head up the stairs to fight your way through another door.

In 3F, Archives 1 has an '''''[[All-Divide]]''''', '''''[[Lemon Gel]]''''', and a chest containing '''''[[Pineapple Gel]]'''''. The Conference Room has a chest with a '''''[[Rune Circlet]]''''', a '''''[[Melange Gel]]''''', and a '''''[[Treat]]'''''. Archives 2 has a chest with '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x8''''', a '''''[[Finesse Ring]]''''', and '''''[[Pearl]] x10'''''. Take the south exit to the Entrance Hall to find '''''[[3500 gald]]'''''

Approach the 4F door for a fight. Those butterflies are surprisingly tough. Now is the best time to leave if you need anything. You know what's coming.

====BOSS BATTLE #12====
@r|SVRFzFwo9Rw
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Nachtigal]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 36)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  28000 |c      1501 |c      1536 |c      1148 |c      1102 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  40000 |c      2059 |c      2109 |c      1642 |c      1576 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  60000 |c      2430 |c      2490 |c      1969 |c      1891 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 100000 |c      2989 |c      3064 |c      2463 |c      2364 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 160000 |c      3918 |c      4019 |c      3284 |c      3152 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water, Earth                                              |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

You have a Dark Cape from this very dungeon; equip it on whoever you think needs it the most. Also, you can steal an Amethyst from him, which you ought to equip immediately. He really likes darkness.

One of the things he likes to do is impale and toss you to the ground. He's also capable of cursing you, so, like always, Elize is a good idea. It's also a good idea to have at least one caster in the back, that way your party isn't taken out all at once.

At times, he'll change his blade to one emanating darkness, and his attacks will pack more of a punch. Then, when he's in overlimit, he'll try spamming Tyrant Spear to try and hit you with his Mystic Arte. STAY. BACK. Luckily, this doesn't hit everyone; just whoever happens to be in reach -- but beware, if everyone is in front of him, they're all as good as dead. (Drache only had Leia survive once. Guess who had the Amethyst equipped.) If everyone gets bunched together, RUN. That should get your linked partner to follow you, at least, which will spare part of your team from potential annihilation. Make sure to set the strategies to keep your frail allies away.

He can cast some artes; if you're ready for them, you can simply run out of their range. He can also stab his sword into the ground; while that attack can follow you, it's fairly easy to also run away from.

|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  21000 |c      1300 |c      1158 |c       765 |c       818 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  30000 |c      1858 |c      1697 |c      1094 |c      1212 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  45000 |c      2229 |c      2056 |c      1312 |c      1474 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  75000 |c      2787 |c      2596 |c      1641 |c      1868 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 120000 |c      3717 |c      3495 |c      2188 |c      2525 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Wind                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Earth                                                     |

Finally, a true three on four battle. Don't overuse casters; you want one caster (probably Elize for healing) and three people to be (mostly) bait. The problem with casters is that they'll probably be targeted in the middle of casting, making them useless. Focus on Jiao; he's definitely the most dangerous and the most obnoxious. He is capable of healing, somehow, so you'll need to seriously use your best wind attacks toward the end.

Note that these people can link. When one overlimits, the other can Mystic Arte away, so try to stay on the unlinked one and let the AI get murdered instead. And if one overlimits alone... again, let the AI be murdered. Fairy Circle (Milla/Elize and Milla/Leia) is actually quite helpful, as it whittles down Jiao's health and keeps up your own. But you're stuck in place, so beware using it.

The worst part? They can confuse you. Try to keep Dispel up. (That arte is simply divine. Elize is always welcome to the party.)

Try to spam your own Mystic Artes in this battle; you need to be in overlimit, then use an Arcane Arte (you probably only have a few, at this point) and holds X. They're increasingly going to go into Overlimit as they die; be patient, don't rush, and you can survive the Mystic Arte hell.

...And now a light based boss with a crap ton of attack. He has some lovely beam attacks, as well as one that wraps around him. He also likes Beast, which knocks you down, and multi-hit sword attacks. Like other bosses, he'll use Mystic Artes, and thus you should RUUUUN when he overlimits. He only hits the people in range, but it will kill whoever gets caught. As he dies, his attacks get crazier, and he starts to confuse you (jerk!).

Be patient; guard when you have to, try to only use life bottles for your main and best healer, and only approach when it's relatively safe. This battle is something of a slog, or maybe even a war of attrition, but only because he hits hard.

===Sillea Tundra (Milla)===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[4000 gald]]           '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Penguinist]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Heart Eyepatch]]      '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Frost Beak]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Pearl]] x8            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Ice Harpy]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Seaweed Salad (Small)]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Snow Treant]]                     '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Omega Elixir]]        '' |c-4 [_] |c-4 '' [[Stalwart Captain]]                '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Jasmine]]         '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Lemon Gel]]           '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Sage]]            '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Milla Wakes]]'''''
+

Whether you go north or south, you'll find the party.

Follow the south wall to '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. Northeast of there, on a tree, is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Heart Eyepatch]]''''', and right behind it is '''''[[Pearl]] x8'''''. Go back to the other wall and follow it south to '''''[[Seaweed Salad (Small)]]''''', and continue south for a scene. You'll be taken to the '''North Region''' automatically.

Head south along the west wall; on the boulder is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Omega Elixir]]'''''. Up the cliff is '''''[[Red Jasmine]]'''''. Just south of the second cliff is '''''[[Lemon Gel]]''''', and southwest of there, along the wall, is '''''[[Red Sage]]'''''. Now you can go where you're supposed to.

===Nala Lava Tubes (Milla)===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures            |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Miracle Gel]]         ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Bat]]                        '' |
|c   [_] |c ''[[Skill Tome: "Wall of Soul"]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Djinn]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Savory]]          ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Golem]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Specific]]            ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Hawk]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Iron Leggings]]       ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Technician Captain]]              '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Gothic Cardigan]]     ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Magma Scorpion]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c ''[[Spicy Chicken Roll (Small)]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Teagle]] (!)                 '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x4''    |c-8 [_] |c-8 '' [[Tiny Teagle]]                     '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[10000 gald]]          ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Saffron]]             ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]]           ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Monster Fluid]] x5    ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Silver Ore]] x20      ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]] x2      ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Flame Cape]]          ''    |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** Up the cliff: '''''[[The Outside World]]''''', '''''[[Cooking with Fire Teagle]]'''''
** After boss: '''''[[An Unexpected Chill]]'''''
+

Gotta love them shops out in the middle of nowhere. Yup.

On the south wall, just after it turns west, is a hole hiding '''''[[Life Bottle]] x2'''''. Follow the path all the way to the west for a '''''[[Miracle Gel]]'''''. On the north path, on the east wall just beyond the vines to climb up, is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Skill Tome: "Wall of Soul"]]'''''. At the end of the path is '''''[[Red Savory]]'''''. Climb up the vines and continue along for a scene and fight. Check the northwest corner of the small area for a hole containing '''''[[Flame Cape]]'''''. Head to the '''Central Region'''.

At the tip of the east path is '''''[[Specific]]'''''. In the west path, on the west wall just north of the loop, is a hole leading to '''''[[Iron Leggings]]'''''. At the fork, head south for a '''''[[Gothic Cardigan]]''''', then head north to come to a '''''[[Spicy Chicken Roll (Small)]]'''''. Climb the vines; on the south wall is a hole with '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x4''''' inside, and, at the end of the path is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[10000 gald]]'''''. Go to the '''Lake Area''' and proceed along the path for a fight. Do equip Barrier Soul on Milla; it's quite handy.

====BOSS BATTLE #15-M====

|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |

He likes to spin around and knock you down, and he summons monsters. All of his attacks are big enough to hit you a backstep away, but that's his biggest quirk. Quite the step down from Gaius, huh? He's not very threatening, even when he steps up the attacks as he dies.

In the '''North Region''', follow the tunnel till it opens up to a wider area and check the east wall for a cavity containing '''''[[Saffron]]''''' along the east wall. Continue to the cliff, then drop down and head all the way west for '''''[[Apple Gel]]'''''. Just east of the vines up, on the south wall, is a hole containing '''''[[Monster Fluid]] x5'''''. Drop down the next cliff and look south for '''''[[Silver Ore]] x20'''''. Leave to the next area.

===Xailen Woods===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Snow Wolf]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Full Frame Glasses]]  '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Ice Golem]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Basil]]           '' |c-3 [_] |c-3 '' [[Tundra Plant]]                    '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Seafood Stew (Small)]]'' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Sephira]]             '' |

For both Jude and Milla, you start at the top of a cliff; the south one for Jude, and the west one for Milla. The following instructions are just from different perspectives.

|* Milla |

Jump down from the cliff and search the south wall for a hole containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Follow the north wall to a boulder; on the other side is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Full-frame Glasses]]'''''. Continue along the north wall for '''''[[Red Basil]]'''''. Then take the east wall south till you find a hole containing '''''[[Seafood Stew (Small)]]'''''. Continue following the wall till you find a second Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Sephira]]'''''.

|* Jude |

At the bottom level, hug search the east wall for Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Sephira]]''''', then continue north along the wall to find a hole containing '''''[[Seafood Stew (Small)]]'''''. By a rock against the north wall is '''''[[Red Basil]]'''''. From there, follow the north wall to the next boulder; on it is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Full-frame Glasses]]'''''. Finally, follow the opposite wall west to a hole containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''.

|* Xailen Woods Temple |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** After reuniting: '''''[[Milla's Sister]]''''' (Jude only), '''''[[Jude's Indiscretion]]'''''
** After meeting with Gaius: '''''[[(A Chat With Wingul)]]''''', '''''[[Footprints]]''''', '''''[[Looking Out for Little Sis]]'''''
** After resting: '''''[[Runs in the Family]]''''', '''''[[The Tao of Jiao]]''''', '''''[[Muzet's Duty]]'''''
+

=--Note...--=
''Do not talk to Wingul.'' You will be able to do that sub event before the final boss, and you'll get a new skit for it.
=-=

Seem familiar? Note that the rest of the party has new armor. Head inside the temple for another scene. Go outside to talk to Agria/Presa for [[Jiao's Demise]]. Rest in the temple (west room Milla; east Jude) to go on. Don't you love how no one uses sheets? There's only once place for you to go, as you can't open any of the doors. Afterward, take the north exit to Kanblar's rooftops.

|* Infiltrating the Ship |
+
|*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Technician Sergeant]]             '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Stalwart Sergeant]]               '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Infiltrator Sergeant]]            '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Spyrix Sentry 1.0]]               '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** After reuniting: '''''[[The Ears of a Monster]]''''', '''''[[(Where Did I Hear of Kanbalar Before)]]''''', '''''[[(Finding the Local Delicacy)]]''''', '''''[[Flying Ships]]'''''
+

Head toward the '''Main Road''' for a scene. It's just a straight path to the castle. A bunch of easy fights ahead. Despite the music, the Spyrix Sentries are regular Guard type enemies. They just happen to have a lot of HP and are stronger than the mooks you just took down.

Afterward, you'll be in Kanbalar. Around the next room in the castle are two scenes (different for both main characters). Exit the castle to find Jude/Milla. Rejoin everyone. DON'T MOVE; if you do, you miss a skit (so Drache believes, anyway). After those (particularly the Local Delicacy skit), head just a little toward the exit again for a scene... and the second part of [[Sisterhood]]. In the Audience Chamber, talk to Wingul for [[Jiao and Wingul]].

Before taking off, head to the inn to find Karla, as the final part of [[The History of Auj Oule]]. In the north room, talk to the guy on the bed for [[Monsters in the Cave]].

If you're on Jude's path, this will send you to the dungeon Milla was just in, and vice versa. In both, you'll be fighting bosses... made easier by having a full party. For Jude, scroll on. For Milla, click [[Kukhar Ice Caverns (Milla)]].

For the plot, talk to Gaius and click [[E.S.S. Zenethra]].

+
+
+

===Nala Lava Tubes (Jude)===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures            |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Miracle Gel]]         ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Bat]]                        '' |
|c   [_] |c ''[[Skill Tome: "Wall of Soul"]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Djinn]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Savory]]          ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Golem]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Specific]]            ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Hawk]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Iron Leggings]]       ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Technician Captain]]              '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Gothic Cardigan]]     ''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Magma Scorpion]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c ''[[Spicy Chicken Roll (Small)]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Fire Teagle]]                     '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x4''    |c   [_] |c   '' [[Tiny Teagle]]                     '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[10000 gald]]          ''    |c-7 [_] |c-7 '' [[Gentlefreet]]                     '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Saffron]]             ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]]           ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Monster Fluid]] x5    ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Silver Ore]] x20      ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]] x2      ''    |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Flame Cape]]          ''    |

To get to the Tubes, climb up the west cliff at Xailen Woods.

Grab the '''''[[Silver Ore]] x20''''' at the south point and climb up the cliff. Hug the south wall to find a hole containing '''''[[Monster Fluid]] x5''''', then head all the way west for an '''''[[Apple Gel]]'''''. Climb the cliff beyond the loop and to the small opening; there, in the north wall, you'll find a cavity containing '''''[[Saffron]]'''''.

At the Lake Area, see [[BOSS BATTLE #15-M]] for any details regarding the Fire Teagle. It should be easy, since you have a full party.


At the '''Central Region''', across from the cliff is '''''[[Spicy Chicken Roll (Small)]]'''''. On top of the cliff, follow the south wall to find a hole with '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x4''''' inside, then head to the end of the path for Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[10000 gald]]'''''. Down the cliff, and to the south point for a '''''[[Gothic Cardigan]]'''''. Continue further along the path, hugging the west wall for '''''[[Iron Leggings]]'''''. Continue towards the exit, but head east, then all the way to the northern tip for a '''''[[Specific]]'''''.

Once you get to the '''South Region''', check the northwest corner of the small area you come to for a hold hiding '''''[[Flame Cape]]'''''. Then jump down the cliff you come and follow the wall north to find Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Skill Tome: "Wall of Soul"]]''''' on the east wall, as well as '''''[[Red Savory]]''''' at the end of the path. Jump down the next cliff to the south and head all the way west for '''''[[Miracle Gel]]'''''. Follow the south wall east for a hole hiding '''''[[Life Bottle]] x2'''''.

Do equip Barrier Soul on Milla; it's quite handy.

|* Sillea Tundra |

|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Sage]]            '' |

Head south along the west wall; on the boulder is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Omega Elixir]]'''''. Up the cliff is '''''[[Red Jasmine]]'''''. Just south of the second cliff is '''''[[Lemon Gel]]''''', and southwest of there, along the wall, is '''''[[Red Sage]]'''''.

At the '''South Region''', follow the south wall to '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. Northeast of there, on a tree, is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Heart Eyepatch]]''''', and right behind it is '''''[[Pearl]] x8'''''. Go back to the other wall and follow it south to '''''[[Seaweed Salad (Small)]]'''''.

To continue with the plot, remember to talk to Gaius and click [[E.S.S. Zenethra]]. And remember to return to the client at Kanbalar's inn.

===Kukhar Ice Caverns (Milla)===

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures          |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[10000 gald]]          ''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Aquadragon 1]]                    '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Aquadragon 2]]                    '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Monster Fluid]] x5    ''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Snow Tortoise]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Takoyaki Ramen (Small)]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Snow Bat]]                        '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Gothic Plate]]        ''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Rime Cat]]                        '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Frost Skeleton]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Treat]]               ''   |c   [_] |c   '' [[Gentlemundine]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Rosy Cheeks]]         ''   |c-5 [_] |c-5 '' [[Ice Mandragora]]                  '' |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Life Bottle]] x2      ''   |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Mushroom Powder]] x7  ''   |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Aqua Cape]]           ''   |
|c   [_] |c   ''[[Iron Leggings]]       ''   |

To get to the Caverns, climb up the south cliff at Xailen Woods.

At the northeast corner of the "8" shape on the map is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[10000 gald]]'''''. Head down the Southern Cliff; at the east end is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6'''''. At the far west end of the map is '''''[[Monster Fluid]] x5'''''.

At the Lake Area, see [[BOSS BATTLE #15-J]] for any details regarding the Aquadragons. It should be easy, since you have a full party.

At the '''Central Region''', go to the north tip for '''''[[Takoyaki Ramen (Small)]]''''', then take the east turn at the end of the path for '''''[[Gothic Plate]]'''''. Follow the south wall to a cavity containing '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Up the cliff, then hug the western wall to come to a hole hiding '''''[[Iron Leggings]]'''''. Now go all the way to the east tip of the path for a '''''[[Treat]]'''''. Then head back and take the first turn south; on the wall there is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Rosy Cheeks]]'''''.

Finally, from the '''South Region''', take the path all the way south to '''''[[Life Bottle]] x2'''''. Up the cliff, down the next, and turn north for '''''[[Mushroom Powder]] x7'''''. Follow the path around the bend and hug the north wall till you find a hole leading to '''''[[Aqua Cape]]'''''.

Exit south to Tulea Tundra.

|* Tulea Tundra |
+
|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Omega Elixir]]        '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[4000 gald]]           '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Saffron]]         '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Peach Pie (Small)]]   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Swordsman's Eyepatch]]'' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5'' |

Follow the west wall; before it turns, you'll come to Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Omega Elixir]]'''''. Just south of there is '''''[[4000 gald]]''''', then continue following along the wall till you find '''''[[Red Saffron]]''''' by a rock. In the '''South Region''', check the northeast corner for '''''[[Peach Pie (Small)]]'''''. On a tree southwest of the Memory Ring is Aifread's Treasure '''''[[Swordsman's Eyepatch]]''''', and along the east wall near the exit is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''.

To continue with the plot, remember to talk to Gaius. And remember to return to the client at Kanbalar's inn.

===E.S.S. Zenethra===

|*+6 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                                                                              |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                 |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Treat]]               ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Resistance Emblem]]   ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Bee's Nest]] x11      ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Stalwart Commander]]              '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Miracle Gel]]         ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x6''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Rare Metal]] x8       ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Infiltrator Commander]]           '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Blue Sage]]           ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[3000 gald]]           ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Everbloom]] x7        ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Technician Commander]]            '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Holy Bottle]] x2      ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Croquette Parfait (Small)]]'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Reverse Doll]]        ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Gun Bee]]                         '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Rotten Bone]] x15     ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Orange Gel]] x2       ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Dark Bottle]]         ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Mechanical Golem]]                '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Sacred Helm]]         ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Jasmine]]             ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5''      |c-7 [_] |c-7 '' [[Silver Bacura]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[3000 gald]]           ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Beetle Leg]] x7       ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Phoenix Ribbon]]      ''      |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Melange Gel]] x2      ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Amulet]]              ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Heavy Treat]]         ''      |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Blue Savory]]         ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Pineapple Gel]]       ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Omega Elixir]]        ''      |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Verbena]]         ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Syrup Bottle]] x2     ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Bizarre Clump]] x5    ''      |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Venomous Stinger]]    ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Elixir]]              ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Life Bottle]]         ''      |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Apple Gel]] x2        ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[4000 gald]]           ''      |c   [_] |c   '' [[Specific]]            ''      |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[Aboard the Zenethra]]''''', '''''[[On the Trail of the Four]]''''', '''''[[Milla the Conflicted]]''''', '''''[[Elympions]]'''''
+

It is possible to find a Silver Bacura here.

If you're on Jude's side, you will automatically find the Technician Captain and Stalwart Captain enemies for the first time. Milla's side featured them a while back.

At least the game never leaves you without supplies. At the '''Central Deck''' is a fight. Afterward, you get a '''''[[Radio]]''''' and '''''[[Zenethra Map]]'''''. This is... quite the ship. You're on the middle/second layer of the ship. To the west of the entrance is a '''''[[Treat]]''''', and the southeast corner has '''''[[Miracle Gel]]'''''. Head to the '''Central Hall''' for a scene, then head down the stairs for '''''[[Holy Bottle]] x2''''' and '''''[[Blue Sage]]'''''. Exit south to ''Starboard Area 1''.

|* Starboard Area 1 |

Periodically, you will hear the enemy talking about defending the port or starboard sides. More enemies will appear at those times; that's your best chance to fight a Golem.

Just next to the entrance is '''''[[Rotten Bone]] x15'''''. Along the main path, take the south stairs and pop outside for '''''[[Sacred Helm]]''''', then continue along the main path till you get to '''''[[3000 gald]]'''''. Next to the east exit is '''''[[Melange Gel]] x2'''''. Go to ''Area 2''. Follow the path the end for '''''[[Blue Savory]]''''' and a door. Inside the Stateroom is '''''[[Venomous Stinger]]''''' in a drawer and '''''[[Red Verbena]]''''' in a chest. Back to Area 1, take the lower south exit for '''''[[Apple Gel]] x2''''', then to warp to the Port side.

Once there, get the '''''[[Resistance Emblem]]''''' and exit to '''Port Area 1'''. Head west; eventually you'll come to the door leading to the starting area and '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x6'''''. Now back down the stairs, and take the lower path east. Take the south fork for '''''[[3000 gald]]''''', and south of the exit is '''''[[Croquette Parfait (Small)]]'''''.

|* Port Area 2 |

Go to the end of the southern corridor is '''''[[Orange Gel]] x2''''', then enter the west Stateroom room for '''''[[Jasmine]]''''' in a chest and '''''[[Beetle Leg]] x7''''' in the shelves.  In the neighboring room is '''''[[Amulet]]'''''. Continue to '''Area 3'''.

Skip the first door; you'll come back. Go all the way east for a '''''[[Pineapple Gel]]''''', and check the shelves in the nearby room for '''''[[Syrup Bottle]] x2'''''. Go to the far east door, the '''Port Engine Room''' for a scene and '''''[[Elixir]]'''''. Outside, head west and take the north door. You can grab one of the boxes; make a path with it to '''''[[4000 gald]]'''''. Now head for '''Area 1'''. Claim the '''''[[Bee's Nest]] x11''''' and head outside for a '''''[[Rare Metal]] x8'''''. Back in Area 3, head for the southwest door you skipped: the '''Port Lounge'''. Take '''''[[Everbloom]] x7''''' from a cupboard and '''''[[Reverse Doll]]''''' from a chest, then warp to Starboard.

|* Starboard Area 3 |

In the Starboard Lounge, claim '''''[[Dark Bottle]]''''' from a cupboard and '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''''' in a chest. Outside to '''Area 3'''.

Stateroom 2, located to in Area 2 to the west of where you are, does not have treasure, but check it for loot if you want. Instead, look at the east end of the Area 3 corridor for '''''[[Phoenix Ribbon]]''''', then check around the nearby Stateroom 4 to the east for a '''''[[Heavy Treat]]''''' in the shelves. Swing around to the south side and enter the '''Starboard Engine Room''' for a scene. Back in Area 3, follow the corridor to Stateroom 3; move the one moveable box inside to get '''''[[Omega Elixir]]'''''. Then head to Area 2 for '''''[[Bizarre Clump]] x5''''', and to the deck for '''''[[Life Bottle]]'''''.

Now, make your way aaaalllllllll the way back to the other side of the ship. Stop at the supply/rest place if you need to. In the area beyond the bars, the '''Central Deck''', is a '''''[[Specific]]'''''. As for the Control Room...

Focus on Gilland first to get him out of the way (though Celsius will protect him at times, so beware). He has a very damaging beam attack that will probably wipe you out if you wind up in right front of it.

Celsius naturally has a variety of ice attacks; one surrounds her to knock you over, and she likes to follow that up with an attack exclusively for downed allies. She also inflicts a bunch of status effects.

They can also perform linked arts, which hit like a truck. Despite all that, they're not difficult so long as you focus on Gilland. Celsius has an Aquamarine to steal/equip, if you don't have one already.

===Hamil (Jude)===

%
====BOSS BATTLE #17====
@r|k5_22jsGxqE
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Alvin]]'''''                                                 '''(LV. 48)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   9800 |c      1117 |c      1272 |c      1253 |c      1203 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  14000 |c      1640 |c      1819 |c      1792 |c      1720 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  21000 |c      1988 |c      2182 |c      2149 |c      2062 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  35000 |c      2510 |c      2729 |c      2688 |c      2580 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  56000 |c      3381 |c      3639 |c      3584 |c      3440 |

You can equip a Reverse Doll, which you should have gotten in the previous dungeon. Alternatively, there's Black Onyx, Amulet (burn sucks), or Stun Talisman. Black Onyx is probably the least useful, but it can help you out of a pinch. Alternatively, you can try Stun Bracelet and Syrup Bottle together, and only equip the Reverse Doll or Black Onyx when you get caught in a combo or a tough spot.

Be warned -- he hits like a TRUCK. You will need to abuse free run and snap pivot if you want to survive. Try to free run around shots (if you see them coming) and snap pivot his sword swings. You can also approach him after he finishes attacking, but be careful. Use a knockdown attack, such as Beast, if you need to heal up. Ideally, don't get hit. Seriously, one of his combos can bring you down. Do use Steel; every bit of attack will help.

Toward the end, he'll heal himself using Guardian Field. Once he starts pulling that, consider spamming Demon Fist to prevent him from getting a full heal out of it.

====BOSS BATTLE #18-J====
@r|7ETrIFw2jMk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (1)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 50)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  33600 |c      2030 |c      1778 |c      2076 |c      1688 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  48000 |c      2901 |c      2542 |c      2967 |c      2414 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  72000 |c      3481 |c      3050 |c      3561 |c      2896 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 120000 |c      4352 |c      3813 |c      4451 |c      3621 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 192000 |c      5803 |c      5085 |c      5935 |c      4828 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Light                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

You'll want Leia and Jude (or just Jude!) up front, so Rowen and Elize can hang back and do what they do best.

Muzet hits pretty hard, including behind her, so you will take quite the beating. You should be a little patient when approaching her, or else don't constantly link with a partner so they don't keep trying (and failing) to match your movements.

She also looooves ailments, so keep Dispel up. Her darkness spells tend to hold you in place or draw you in, so do your best to stay clear of those.

Once she overlimits, she'll spam long range magic suddenly... Block the stuff that follows you, if you can't run around it in time, and run away from any spells. One of your allies is sure to be dumb enough to get hit by her Mystic Arte, so keep your health way up, and use whatever you need to survive.

===Spirit Realm (Milla)===

^l17|

|*+2 Items / Equipment / Treasures         |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                                  |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x5'' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Coastal Mandragora (Spirit Realm)]]         '' |

You can find Silver Bacura, probably in any of these regions. Not the kind of fun to have on your own.

What are you wearing, Milla? (Not to mention her hair is worse than usual.) Talk to the spirits twice, then try to leave for a scene. Climb the west cliff to the '''West Beach'''. The chests should be familiar to you, but I will cover them again. Climb up the two cliffs, then down the south ones for '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5'''''. Continue to the area by the Memory Ring, then take the trail east to '''''[[Sharp Pincers]] x11'''''. You can enter Nia Khera if you wish, to talk to the people there and listen to the spirits talk (it's interesting!), but head back to '''Below Falls''', then '''Central Area'''.

If we're in the Spirit Realm, does that mean we can pay with Spirit money? No? Darn. You can buy stuff from the shop, here by some miracle. Across from him, in the wall, is '''''[[French Toast (Large)]]'''''. Up the cliffs, then check the northwest for '''''[[Giant Fish Fin]] x6'''''. Head to the southeast side of the raised area and jump down to the chest containing '''''[[Apple Gel]] x3'''''. To '''East Beach'''.

Up the cliff and take the south way around to a '''''[[Blue Rosemary]]'''''. Jump down the following two cliffs and check next to the water for '''''[[Paladin's Cape]]'''''.

====BOSS BATTLE #18-M====
@r|HOansGUaDeI
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (2)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 50)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |

|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

You should have a Rebirth Doll from the Zenethra. If you feel like you're going to die, equip it. Black Onyx can also be used if you get snagged in a combo, but it's less reliable since it only increases your HP.

She capable of many status ailments, so use Syrup Bottles or an Amulet. If you back off of her, she'll attempt to attack you from underground or cast a wind/dark/fire spell. The Four, naturally, are good attacks to use once you start staggering her, as well as any light attacks you have (Drache used Divine Streak; do spam it if you're in a tight spot, it's wonderful). The best way to handle her is hit and run... or guard, but be careful, as she can break it fairly easily. She can throw you, regardless of whether you're guarding, and she can attack in all directions. Once she overlimits, she'll spam long range magic suddenly... Block the stuff that follows you, if you can't run from it in time, and run away from any spells. Her Mystic Arte will reduce you to 1 HP. Avoid the black ball; it holds you in place. The black things on the ground also draw you to them, so stay far away.

The major problem with her is that a couple combos may be enough to kill you. The easiest times to attack her are after she tries her underground stabby attack, when she taunts you, and when she passes through you. If you're close enough, you should be able to nail her before she casts a spell too. You can also try knocking her down with a Flare Bomb if you need a short breather.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items'' |
|c   20000 |c     5000 |c [[Mystic Emblem]] |

Climb up two cliffs. At the southern tip is  a hole leading to '''''[[Specific]]''''', and at the northern tip is a hole leading to '''''[[Hourglass]]'''''. Climb the vines near the north hole to reach the top. Collect the '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x5''''' to the south before moving on to the '''Halfway Point'''.

On the second cliff of that area, at the north point, is a hole leading to '''''[[Red Lavender]]'''''. Climb to the top layer to find a hole in front of you leading to '''''[[Creamy Beef Bowl (Small)]]''''' and '''''[[4000 gald]]''''' further along the path. Continue to the '''Summit'''.

Everyone has better equipment now.

====BOSS BATTLE #21====
@r|mnFmWnVVNpI
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Maxwell]]'''''                                               '''(LV. 60)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  49000 |c      2724 |c      2044 |c      2324 |c      2212 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  70000 |c      3720 |c      2920 |c      3320 |c      3160 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c 105000 |c      4384 |c      3504 |c      3984 |c      3792 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 175000 |c      5380 |c      4380 |c      4980 |c      4740 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 280000 |c      7040 |c      5840 |c      6640 |c      6320 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Variable; opposite of strength                            |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Variable                                                  |

Coming from Jude's side, a scene will happen a little into the battle, then another after his Mystic Arte, and yet another after a second one! Theeeennnn the party really starts. And the butthole's HP is reset.

He's a little hard to knock down and has big attacks. You'll notice Maxwell uses variations of attacks Milla has, so you should generally know what his attacks do; knockdown from fire, hold in place with darkness, and so on. The biggest problem is that the jerkface steals your TP, so you may want to use Treats. His Mystic Arte will hit the entire party, but it isn't devastating (especially with all elemental resistances up).  He's really not that difficult and should go down fairly easily.

The great thing about Milla is that she hits about every weakness, making her great for this battle... not to mention the Four are quite broken, if costly.

This boss likes to bounce and roll around the field, zap all around himself, and zap whoever is in front of him. He's shockingly easy, pun intended. Even when he starts going all out or in overlimit, he's not at all hard.

How to make this battle hilariously easy: Equip Elemental Guard (resists Fire/Water/Earth/Wind) and Dragon Helm (resists Fire) or find a good equivalent. Then combine with Fire/Wind Guard skills. You will ABSORB most of Volts attacks.

North of the entrance, by a tree, is '''''[[Red Saffron]]''''', then check the wall east of there for a hole containing '''''[[Treat]]'''''. Continue following the wall north to come to a '''''[[Heavy Treat]]''''' amidst trees. The wall west of there has a hole leading to '''''[[Miracle Gel]]'''''.

In the '''Central Region''', follow the south wall; as it turns north, you'll find a cavity with '''''[[Lemon Gel]] x3''''' inside. Check the wall just a little more north of there to find Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Collar]]'''''. Just west of there, by a rock, is '''''[[Guardian Symbol]]''''', then follow the west wall north till you see a tree with '''''[[Pot au Feu (Large)]]''''' by it. At the '''North Region''', head north from the entrance; near a tree by the north wall is '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x4'''''. Hug the north wall from there and head west for a hole hiding '''''[[Migrant Plume]] x7'''''. Further west, by a tree, is '''''[[6000 gald]]''''', and on the next tree west from there (near the exit) is Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Rare Boots]]'''''. Near a few trees by the opposite wall is '''''[[Meadow Crystal]] x6'''''. There is a boss monster near here; you'll be directed to it shortly.

Enter the '''Tatalian Abyss''' exit to create a shortcut. We'll direct you there after some plot. Instead, head to the northeast exit to the '''Dimensional Breach'''.

Skit obsessed? Don't beat Dranzort at Tatalian Abyss till you've beaten any other Devil's Beast (except Melanbron). There are two versions of the skit: one for Jude, one for Milla.

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:

Then, as the skit suggests, turn around and head in the Mathis Clinic for [[The Aspyrixis]]. Head to the '''Old Vicalle Mine''' now; the boy is at the North Region.

You can fight the Devil's Beast Roparde while you're in the Mine, but it has a quirk -- it summons four Fili-type monsters representing each element. Which he summons depends on what his elemental strength is at the time he calls for help, so let use Barrier Change every so often (and hit him with his weakness to trigger it? Maybe?). You want to see all of them for your enemy data; be soft on him till he summons all four.

After saving the boy, check the counter by the Food Vendor for the final part of [[Memories of Leronde]].

|c   [_] |c   '' [[Technician Veteran]]              '' |

*NEW SKITS AVAILABLE:
** '''''[[(A Dialogue Between Worlds)]]''''', '''''[[(That's a Big House)]]''''', '''''[[(Let's Go Visit Driselle)]]''''', '''''[[(Finding the Light-Leaf Clover)]]''''', '''''[[(And Back to Balan Once More)]]'''''
+

At '''Trigleph''', STOP. Get the first skit listed, and you might as well get the second as well. You can move now.

There is an automatic scene in the Commercial District, which is part of [[Love-Fevered Visions]]. Head to 3F of Rodo Apartments for the final part of [[Sisterhood]], then talk to Balan for [[Balan's Bet]]. At '''Rusalle Highroad - North Region''', pretty much in the middle of the path between all exits, is a golden/sparkly patch of plants to inspect. After the fight, return to Balan.

From the Torbalan entrance of '''Helioborg Fortress''', head inside the building for [[The Origin of Spyrite]]. While you're here, you can fight the Devil's Beast, Melanbron, on the roof where you fought Volt... but if you're skit obsessed, don't do it unless you've killed Roparde, Gartrega, Schweiss, or Folzam first.

Now back to Driselle in '''Sharilton''' for the final part of [[Love-Fevered Visions]].

If you are skit obsessed, you will miss a skit if you fight Dranzort (the Tatalian Abyss monster) or Melanbron first.

|* Mysterious Jewel Bosses |

Now you should kill those two boss monsters you may have passed by in Elympios -- they drop Mysterious Jewels.

* [[Veywind Eye]]
** Go to '''Torbalan Highroad - Central Region'''.
** He likes to stun you and he can petrify you so BEWARE.
+
* [[Graddic Claw]]
** Located at '''Rasalle Highroad - Tatalian Abyss Entrance'''.

|* Kanbalar |

Head toward the castle for [[Gaius, the King]]. You can also talk to Wingul for [[The Two Generals]], if you didn't do it in Chapter 3.

Seriously, do [[Tatalian Abyss]] right now if you haven't. Otherwise you're not getting far in the coming sub event.

At Xailen Woods Temple, head inside the building and continue forward for a scene. The Mysterious Jewels you've been collecting DO have a purpose -- give it all the jewels you have (you should have all 23 now!). This is for [[The Lost Transcendental Ring]].

Immediately after giving it all 23 Jewels, you're launched into an easy boss fight against [[Crimson Servant]] and [[Azure Servant]]. (Make 'em even easier? Equip a Blue Cape. You'll absorb all the darkness attacks.) You get '''''[[Arte Tome: "One-Hit Kill"]]''''' for the trouble.

===Tatalian Abyss===

|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures                                                                  |*+2 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Magical Ore]] x7             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Strange Core]] x2            '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Twilight Sentinel]]               '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Copper Ore]] x20             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[10000 gald]]                 '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Lizardman]]                       '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Creepy Antenna]] x6          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Mysterious Jewel]]           '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Blade Beak]]                      '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Ancient Coral]] x8           '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Jet Black Feather]] x10      '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Dranzort]]                        '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Sapphire Shell]] x5          '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Dragon Ash]] x3              '' |c-4 [_] |c-4 '' [[Burrow Goblin]]                   '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Superhero Belt]]             '' |c   [_] |c   '' [[Blue Sephira]]               '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Hair of the Sacred Beast]] x5'' |c-2 [_] |c-2 '' [[Omega Elixir]]               '' |
|c   [_] |c   '' [[Red Sage]]                   '' |

You can find Pink Emeralds here to finally complete [[Pretty and Pink]]. At long last, Elize can be a Pro Pinkist.

You may also find Gold Bacuras here.

=--Note...--=
This place is pretty good for grinding up shop levels. There are a lot of good materials to gather here, like [[Pink Emerald]] and [[Dingy Puffball]]. But more importantly, the enemies have good items. Blade Beaks drop [[Pheasant Tail]], and it's their stealable item as well. They're by far the best enemy to fight for materials. Twilight Sentinels drop [[Libavius Ore]] (like the Goblins do), but more importantly, you can steal [[Dragon Ash]] from them.
=-=

Take the southwest path to '''''[[Magical Ore]] x7''''', then follow the main path to a scene. This is part of [[The Gathering Miasma]]. Before proceeding, check the north point of the area behind you for '''''[[Copper Ore]] x20'''''. Jump down the cliff and turn around to find '''''[[Creepy Antenna]] x6'''''. Continue toward the floaty object for a scene. As it suggests, jump!

|* B1F |

Head toward the wind seal, then to the northwest region for '''''[[Ancient Coral]] x8''''' on a small cliff. In the area west of there is '''''[[Sapphire Shell]] x5'''''.

Now go to the southeast wing, and take the north path. Behind a few boxes on the west wall is an Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Superhero Belt]]'''''. Continue northwest for a ladder; climb it, take the '''''[[Hair of the Sacred Beast]] x5''''', and jump on the earth seal from the nearby cliff.

|* B2F |

Take the northeast path and climb up the cliffs to a '''''[[Red Sage]]''''', and further along the path, take the southeast fork to break the wind seal. Head back to the main path, and climb up the nearby cliff. From there, go up a series of small cliffs to the northeast to find '''''[[Strange Core]] x2'''''. You are now in the same area as the earth seal; drop down to ground level and climb the northern cliffs to stomp on the earth seal.

|* B3F |

Take the northwest path, then the northeast branch to the wind seal and '''''[[10000 gald]]'''''. When you crawl back out of that area, Aifread's Treasure, '''''[[Mysterious Jewel]]''''', should be directly ahead of you.

You should have all 61 Treasures now. If you fought Veywind Eye and Graddic Claw, you should have 23 Mysterious Jewels. Otherwise, 21.

Head back to the entrance and take the southeast path to '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10''''' in the easternmost point, then climb the cliffs to the northwest for '''''[[Dragon Ash]] x3'''''. Jump down to smash the earth seal. From the entrance, take the northwest path and the northwest branch to arrive near a cliff you can climb up for '''''[[Blue Sephira]]'''''.

|* Depths |

Claim the '''''[[Omega Elixir]]''''' and proceed... to Dranzort, a Devil's Beast. Drache was around level 63 for this fight. Just keep him out of the range of your healer(s), guard when you see the attack coming (they're big and slow), maybe take Alvin since he can take a hit, and you'll be fine. You'll get '''''[[Dranduo, the Howling Beast]]''''', for your trouble.

If you have any unfinished sub events ([[Pretty and Pink]], [[The Lost Transcendental Ring]], [[The Devil's Beasts]]), remember to finish them.

+

He's lightning fast, making him a pain to combo (and to keep off your healer/caster), and he breaks out of combos easier than before. His favorite getaway attack is Rising Phoenix, and he's also quite fond of Severing Wind to make you back off. Later in the battle, he's start casting short range spells; do make sure you have Elize for this part, as the ailments start popping up.

Want to make it easy? Just equip your best wind resistant stuff.

Unlike his counterpart, Gaius packs a punch. He's quite fond of knockdown attacks, and his combos are pretty likely to kill you. Knock him down if you need to heal up. If you equip a Red Cape,  you'll be immune to his light based attacks. Snap Pivot is your very best friend.

When he approaches the halfway point, he'll get SUPER CHEAP with Swallow Fury. But you can survive it, and he won't spam it all the time.

====BOSS BATTLE #25====
@r|zOAr5J8c4sk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Gaius (3)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 70)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  84000 |c      1812 |c      1873 |c      2142 |c      1261 |
|c ''Normal''             |c 120000 |c      3233 |c      3190 |c      3275 |c      2317 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c 180000 |c      4179 |c      4068 |c      4030 |c      3020 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 300000 |c      5599 |c      5385 |c      5162 |c      4075 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 480000 |c      7966 |c      7581 |c      7050 |c      5834 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Dark                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Light                                                     |
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (4)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 70)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  37800 |c      1535 |c      1397 |c      1392 |c      1584 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  54000 |c      2751 |c      2511 |c      2633 |c      2777 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  81000 |c      3561 |c      3253 |c      3458 |c      3573 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 135000 |c      4777 |c      4366 |c      4699 |c      4766 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 216000 |c      6802 |c      6222 |c      6766 |c      6755 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Light                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

Together, they'll mow you over; rely on your cheapest tactics possible -- running! Gradually, your party will rejoin and use their Mystic Artes. Just focus on surviving till you get a full party.

Like for other bosses, you can abuse elemental resistances. Start out with Amethyst, Elemental, Diamond, and such, as well as your best armor that resists either Light/Dark. Don't pull out Red/Blue Cape till one of them is gone. Beware: Muzet casts Sunburst.

Note that Muzet's health is a LOT lower. But it's hard to beat her down; she'll auto-revive once in the battle, and that's if she doesn't otherwise heal up first. Apparently she heals when she guards, so make sure to break it using Beast or something. Consider using an Hourglass if you have too much trouble with her. Otherwise, Muzet's not really all that different from the other times you fought her; she's more tedious than difficult.

Do not beat Gaius first; Muzet can revive him to half health. Put EVERYTHING into taking Muzet down.

One thing they're capable of is stopping time (like an Hourglass), then pummeling you. Do your best to not get right between them; they'll rip you apart. Gaius is good at shredding, but he's actually not too bad till he gets super-fast at the halfway point. At this point, Elize should have Revive and Leia should have good item skills, so use them both as necessary.

Oh yes. Do STEAL from both of them so they can't use their items. Muzet is particularly obnoxious with Treat spamming.

On Milla's path, you get '''''[[Spirit Garb (Milla)]]''''' and '''''[[Spirit Hairstyle (Milla)]]'''''.

On Jude's, you get '''''[[Medical Outfit (Jude)]]'''''.

For both, you receive '''''[[Arte Tome: "Tremorous Fist"]]''''', '''''[[Arte Tome: "Spirit Surge"]]''''', and '''''[[Golden Key]]'''''.

If you use the Arcane Artes you got from those tomes, Milla and Jude can use their dual Mystic Arte, Tiger Blade Sigma.

Since you have the Golden Key, you can now head to the bonus dungeon, [[Magnus Zero]]. Enter '''Fezebel Marsh''' from the Arklund Quag entrance and head all the way in. This starts [[The Golden Mage Knight]].

===Magnus Zero===

|*+4 Monster / Bestiary Entries                        |

|c   [_] |c   '' [[Temporal Sentinel]]               '' |


Every five levels, there's an blue orb general shop (everything but an item shop), exit column of light, and Memory Ring. There are treasures here, and they aren't randomized. They're nice to pick up, and some hold equipment, but ultimately you can get the items elsewhere. Still, this place is great for material grinding.

Seriously, Leia should be your best friend here for stealing, and be sure to gather a lot.

|* Fennmont to Sapstrath Deepwood  (1F - 5F) |
+
|*+4 Items / Equipment / Treasures               |

'''Fennmont'''
: Behind you is '''''[[10000 gald]]''''', and '''''[[Blue Sage]]''''' is at the southernmost tip of the area. Exit through the north warp.

'''Labari Hollow'''
: North across the bridge is '''''[[Blue Savory]]'''''. near the entrance of the area is a '''''[[Demon Seal]]''''', and the warp is further along the path.

'''Sillea Tundra'''
: There is a tree to the west of the exit; next to it is '''''[[Specific]]'''''. Just to the west of the nearest cliff from there is '''''[[Blue Rosemary]]'''''. Climb the west cliff for '''''[[Enchanted Thorns]] x9''''' and take the nearby exit.

'''Kanbalar'''
: There is '''''[[Lemon Gel]] x3''''' at the north side of the central circle, '''''[[Eye of the Demon Beast]] x8''''' in the southeast notch, and '''''[[Blue Lavender]]''''' in the south hall. Take the north exit.

'''Sapstrath Deepwood'''
: Go south to find a '''''[[Strength Ring]]''''', then crawl through the hole and go up the vines. Here, there is a way out, a Memory Ring, and all shops except the Item Shop.

|* Galia Trail to Helioborg Fortress (6F - 10F) |

'''Galia Trail'''

: Along the south wall right next to where you start is '''''[[Pheasant Tail]] x6'''''. To the opposite wall and follow it to the north to reach '''''[[Life Bottle]] x3''''', and continue along it for a '''''[[Blue Chamomile]]''''' in the northwest corner. Take the WEST exit.

'''Felgana Mine'''

: Go all the way to the southwest corner for '''''[[Pineapple Gel]] x3'''''. By the warp to the north is '''''[[10000 gald]]''''', and at the northeast corner is '''''[[Demon Bug Eye]] x8'''''. Take the small passages south to reach the south exit.

'''Xagut Floodmeadow'''

: Along the east wall is '''''[[French Toast (Medium)]]'''''. On the opposite wall is a hole leading to '''''[[Jet Black Feather]] x10'''''. Jump down the cliff; at the bottom of the second one is '''''[[Dingy Puffball]] x10'''''. Take either warp.

'''Sharilton'''

%

If you want to know what Drache did... she had her typical boss beating party up, which was like this:

* Milla - Good to have linked to Jude. Otherwise can be replaced by Alvin.
* Jude - Linked to Milla for all the Linked Artes and Tiger Blade Sigma. He's a generally good link partner and distraction if you need one.
* Leia - Heal/First Aid disabled. She's a good distraction for one of the Knights Can generally be replaced with Alvin, but she works better linked to Elize than the melee characters do.
* Elize - Pixie Circle/Recover/Healing Circle disabled. Largely used for Nurse and Revive, very occasional dark magic.
* Rowen - Whenever the occasion popped up that he could be used without being destroyed by one of the Mage Knights. Usually quickly switched out for Leia.

It also took her half an hour at level 70-75. Longer on Unknown in the low 80's, but she decided to goof off at the end and experiment with weaknesses just for all of you.

...Still need help? Very well, here is the most game-breaking advice possible. Here's the equipment you should have... for anyone except Alvin:

* ''Headgear:'' [[Elemental Circlet]] (Ladies) / [[Wizard's Hat]] or [[Divine Miter]] (Jude) / [[Tactician's Hat]] (Rowen)
* ''Armor:'' [[Elemental Guard]] / [[Shining Coat]] (Milla) / [[Tactician's Coat]] (Rowen) / [[Rose Dress]] or [[Elemental Cloak]] (Elize)
* ''Accessory:'' [[Elemental]] (Jude) / [[Elemental Cape]] (Anyone else)

Combined with linking and all the elemental Guard skills, you will be absorbing most of what comes your way outside of physical attacks. Not quite everything, but this should cover everything but Light/Dark... which will both be weakened a lot anyway.

Alvin has a variety of equipment to work with, but not much with multiple resists. With [[Elemental]] and linking, he can have 90% resist to any element.

Yeeeeep. Two casters now; Puppeteer and Creator. This is going to hurt. The last one, you could have done okay in. This one? People are going to die. There's just no way around it. Milla's spirits are even better here, as they create a fine excuse to attack her over other targets.

The Puppeteer is the worst, though, as it heals and casts. Be prepared to kick its ass quickly. Once it goes down (it will be difficult due to HP fluctuations), the battle will go smoothly. Beast is effective at stopping Healing Circle.

You can take down the Creator first, if you want, but only do so if you have enough Dark resist on everyone so the Puppeteer can be totally ineffective... except for Terror and occasional healing. Otherwise, resist light instead of darkness.

Save the Scholar for last; he hits REALLY hard, and you don't need that on top of the Creator's spells.

Elements... pretty much any resistances would be useful. Puppeteer loves darkness, and the Creator likes to spam everything but water.

===Coliseum===

This is not intended to be something to help you get through an Unknown run of the Coliseum. The fact is, you should be comfortable with a character if you're going to do things "legit".

Turn the difficulty down to Easy; these are simply easy ways to get you through the solo matches, both the Advanced Single and the Grand Master fights. Try to be over level 70, at least.

* ''Jude''
** Shattering Demon Fist is good for hitting a crowd, and Demon Fist is good from a distance. Whirlwind Snap is also fun to spam. It's not as powerful as Shattering Demon Fist, but it doesn't knock the enemy down.
+
* ''Milla''
** Gnome is decent when surrounded, Undine can be used from a distance, and Efreet is just great. If you have the ability to cast in air, then Sunburst everything to oblivion.
+
* ''Alvin''
** Arc Fire and Pulse Shot. Very cheap, but very effective. If you really want to turn your brain off, switch to semi auto and spam Variable Trigger.
+
* ''Elize''
** Teepo Roar for anything stopping you from casting, Negative Gate for everything else. Equip a [[Mystic Emblem]].
+
* ''Rowen''
** Tidal Wave, and Fireball for anyone too fast (Jude or Ivar). Equip a [[Mystic Emblem]] or his Speed Cast skill. For Jude, don't be afraid to use an Hourglass to give you time to cast.
+
* ''Leia''
** Crescent Flash for hitting a crowd. Occasionally Staff Rain, and Darting Claw. Just use whatever sticks for you; she's a little difficult to get used to. Equip Bonus Extension 2 so you can Flash Guard for Elongated Staff.

+
+
+

''Grinding to Level 99''

=-----=

The following information is from Xavalia of GFAQs. It's amazingly effective.

Equip [[Demon Seal]]s on everyone but Rowen, who should have a [[Dark Seal]].

When you go into the Coliseum, your party is "hidden", but is still "participating" in battle. So anyone who is "on the field" will get bonus experience from coliseum fights and everyone else will level up normally as well.

With no experience multipliers, and using [[Spicy Chicken Roll (Large)]], you can get 30,000 experience per each Advanced Singles fight. Each fight lasts about 40 seconds, so it goes much more quickly than any other grinding method.

To make fights go quickly, spam Tidal Wave, preferably with Speed Cast and Grace equipped. That's it. If you don't have his Grace skill yet, you can either try to Fireball Ivar's face off, and/or you can taunt with the Charismatic Stance skill equipped. Neither of them are quite as effective as the Grace skill, but they can get you through.

=-=

===Odds and Ends (Trophy Hunting)===

First of all, scroll through [[Etc. Skits]] to see if you missed anything, aside from gameplay-related skits.

In the event that you don't have some Titles/Trophies related to gameplay, there are some simple tricks you can do. Not all of them are super-fast, sorry.

''Infinite Combo''

=-----=

* ''Milla''
** No linking, set all characters to manual.
** Push enemy against wall, spam Sylph
** Equip [[Risk Ring]], or use Gels when she runs out of TP.
** Minimum Damage skill
** Hilariously easy.

Mega thanks to myfavoritetvsho of GFAQs for pointing out this trick.

=-=

+
+
+

''Special Abilities (Player)''

=-----=
* ''Snap Pivot''
** There's no easy way to do this one; find an enemy you find predictable and start dodging.
+
* ''Spirit Shift''
** Just spam Flare Bomb, Wind Blade, etc. like crazy.
** Skills: Minimum Damage
+
* ''Charge''
** Like Spirit Shift, spam whatever technique you like and hold CIRCLE to charge up each time.
** Skills: Minimum Damage, Speed Charge
+
* ''Teepo Switch''
** Keep hitting L3.
** Recommended Enemy: [[Tortoise]]. It's slow.
** Skills: Do NOT equip Morale Support.
+
* ''Arte Tuning''
** Try pressing O to Wind Lance or Rock Trine. Something quick and easy.
** Skills: Minimum Damage
+
* ''Elongating Staff''
** Even though you are supposed to backstep, Leia's not as good at it as Jude. Instead, Flash Guard. You do not have to wait for the staff to disappear.
** Recommended Enemy: [[Axe Beak]]
** Skills: Flash Guard, Bonus Extension 2

=-=

+
+
+

''AI Skills''

=-----=
* ''Restore''
** [[Cave Plant]] is wonderful. Just walk up to 'em and stand there like a dummy. Switch to Manual control; Semi-Auto makes you auto guard.
+
* ''Bind''
** Be Elize. Pow Hammer stuns, which makes binding extra easy. Probably do it on a Speed type enemy, such as [[Fleet Mare]] to make it easy, but it will work on anything you can stun consistently.
** Skills: Minimum Damage
+
* ''Breaker''
** Find a Guard type enemy, such as a Golem type enemy and turn off all Alvin's artes. Go sort of easy on them to give them a lot of opportunities to block.
** Skills: Minimum Damage
+
* ''Teepo Drain''
** Find a Technical Type enemy, for instance, [[Leafy Mandragora]], and turn off all Elize's artes. She'll drain a lot. She'll drain even more if you can effectively combo in the air. Try spamming Cloud Pierce or something similar. Whatever you do, spam something that costs a good chunk of TP.
** Skills: Minimum Damage
+
* ''Auto Magic Guard''
** Try entering a battle full of Channelers, such as [[Insurgent Channeler]]. Goblin enemies may work as well. As long as you don't move, your AI ally won't either!
+
* ''Item Steal''
** Try to target Gentleman type enemies. They drop [[Dingy Puffball]], which is good for the shops. Otherwise, just pick any enemy that has a stealable item and knock 'em down with your arte of choice.

=-=

+
+

==New Game+ / Grade Shop==

Upon completion of the game, you can save clear data that will allow you to start a new game with bonuses, depending on how many titles you earned during your last playthrough. Each title earned you a set amount of points to use in the Grade Shop! Here's what can be purchased using those points upon starting New Game+.

For most titles, your progress carries on to the next playthrough. So if you still need 800 encounters, for instance, you won't have to start again from zero.

|* Reward                        |* Grade Points |* Description                                                                                                                   |

====BOSS BATTLE #01 ====
@r|nZU5eWdiQ4k
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Girl in Red]]'''''                                           '''(LV. 05)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |r   2100 |r       111 |r       136 |r       117 |r       111 |
|c ''Normal''             |r   3000 |r       161 |r       196 |r       169 |r       159 |
|c ''Moderate''           |r   4500 |r       192 |r       234 |r       202 |r       191 |
|c ''Hard''               |r   7500 |r       241 |r       294 |r       253 |r       239 |
|c ''Unknown''            |r  12000 |r       322 |r       392 |r       338 |r       319 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Wind                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Earth                                                     |

''Part 1:'' This part is for Jude only, leading to it being a two part battle. This first battle you're meant to lose, so go ahead and let her take you out (unless you want a lengthy, meaningless challenge.) The second part of the battle is fought by both regardless of who you're controlling.

''Part 2:'' Milla is super overpowered. Unless you're on a harder difficulty, even if Red staggers you a lot, there shouldn't be a problem mopping the floor with her. If you're not already controlling her, just use L1 and her directional button to take control of her, then spam Sylph or Undine using LEFT STICK + UP (or + RIGHT) to wipe her out. Hopefully you're quick enough and Jude wins some EXP as well.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |
|c     250 |c      500 |

====BOSS BATTLE #02 ====
@r|2-LU1pIinjs
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Greater Demon]]'''''                                         '''(LV. 08)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   9800 |c       271 |c       280 |c       209 |c       197 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  14000 |c       388 |c       402 |c       300 |c       282 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  21000 |c       465 |c       481 |c       359 |c       338 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  35000 |c       582 |c       603 |c       450 |c       424 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  56000 |c       777 |c       804 |c       600 |c       565 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Fire                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Water                                                     |

This boss comes attached to a tutorial about linked artes. You might as well try chaining on this boss, as he isn't particularly difficult at the beginning. His movements start slow enough that you can tell, most of the time, when to guard. He does have two attacks he'll start spamming that both hit a wide circular range; you'd better run if he starts it. He'll thrust his antennas into the ground when he activates either of them; the difference between them is that one attack follows its target (probably you), and the other is short range.

To deal some decent damage, control Milla and use her Fireball in conjunction with either Alvin's Tiger Blade to land Hell Pyre, or Jude's Soaring Vortex for Aerial Fire. (If you have Jude's Steel and Milla's Flame Ring, then that does even more damage, though it's a bit harder to get Jude to cooperate.) Link with Alvin on occasion when he's needed to break the Demon's guard, and use Jude for normal attacks when Milla's TP runs low and he's not needed for healing. Depending on the difficulty, if you don't like playing healer, it's worth it to take control of Milla, since you'll likely be healing more often than not.

One of the cute things about ailments in this game is that if your linked partner gets one, you get one too. So watch out for weak. Oh, and don't be a dummy like Drache was. Upgrade your equipment. ;)

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items'' |
|c    400  |c      800 |c [[Poison Ward]]   |
+
