====BOSS BATTLE #03 ====
@r|lC9CvcwKlbk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Jiao (1)]]'''''                                              '''(LV. 13)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  11900 |c       303 |c       314 |c       259 |c       256 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  17000 |c       435 |c       450 |c       372 |c       368 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  25000 |c       521 |c       539 |c       445 |c       440 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  42500 |c       653 |c       675 |c       557 |c       552 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  68000 |c       871 |c       900 |c       744 |c       736 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Wind                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Earth                                                     |

He comes with two small fry. Be sure to get rid of them quickly so the whole party is focused on the big guy. If Jiao is chasing you, by all means ignore them. He hits like a truck. He's just slow enough to guard when he brings his hammer down to blast the area around him. You'll want to keep Elize's TP up so she can heal.

Definitely control Milla in this fight, as Jude's Soaring Vortex takes too long and keeps you open for damage. Link with him though, as tossing in an extra Final Gale and / or Aerial Fire definitely helps. Do your best to hit him with Milla's wind attacks, as they may actually stagger him. His attacks get heavier as you whittle down his HP, and they tend to either stun or knock you down. He will also summon a [[Hawk]] at some point, as well as another [[Sylvan Wolf]] or two. At this point, it's best to keep Jiao's attention yourself; otherwise he'll beat up the *rest* of your party.

In the event you have access to Fairy Circle (Milla/Elize), don't cast it too close to him unless you want to get stunned after casting. Hammer Rain is pretty good, though.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items'' |
|c    450+ |c    1000+ |c [[Wind Cape]]     |

====BOSS BATTLE #04 ====
@r|AUq3-BJFuzg
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Nameless Anomaly]]'''''                                      '''(LV. 16)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  14000 |c       369 |c       387 |c       329 |c       270 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  20000 |c       529 |c       555 |c       471 |c       388 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  30000 |c       634 |c       665 |c       564 |c       465 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  50000 |c       794 |c       832 |c       706 |c       581 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  80000 |c      1059 |c      1110 |c       942 |c       776 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Earth                                                     |

Consider using Syrup Bottles; they have limited times, but prevent ailments. This guy will inflict a bunch of 'em with mist attacks -- Arteseal, Poison, and Skillseal. He also has wide range, hard hitting attacks (one stuns!), so try to keep him away from Elize if you have her out. Consider giving her (or everyone, depending on how many you have) the Seal Ward so she can keep healing and using artes, and someone else should have the Stun Bracelet on (likely Jude, so he's always dealing damage). He can cast both a bell attack (it can confuse, but this is a larger problem on higher difficulties) or a wind attack, so be sure to stay on him and consider linking to Rowen when you see it coming.

Your best bet is using Igneous Crush (Jude's Cerberus Strike / Milla's & Rowen's Rock Trine) and chaining from there if you're lucky, getting as many in as you can per set of Linked Artes. While it is weak to Earth, Rock Trine on its own will miss most of the time, making it practically useless. You can also spam Fireball (with extra Fireballs) with Rowen from a distance, if you're having trouble.

If you have access to Recovery Heal (Jude's Recovery Ring / Elize's Recover), that would be quite lovely to use this battle, as it acts like a massive Syrup Bottle AND Panacea Bottle. Pixie Heal (Jude's Healer / Elize's Pixie Heal) also works quite nicely for mass HP recovery.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items''                |
|c     600 |c     1000 |c [[Winged Boots]], [[Earth Cape]] |

====BOSS BATTLE #05 ====
@r|mpAre9KXTDw
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Ivar (1)]]'''''                                              '''(LV. 17)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   4900 |c       412 |c       415 |c       333 |c       341 |
|c ''Normal''             |c   7000 |c       590 |c       595 |c       477 |c       488 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  10500 |c       707 |c       713 |c       572 |c       585 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  17500 |c       885 |c       892 |c       716 |c       732 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  28000 |c      1180 |c      1190 |c       955 |c       976 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Earth                                                     |

If you're used to Milla (Drache was!), this is really awkward, but can be done. Aqua Sweep will knock him down and give you time to recover, just make sure to run away from him first. His combos are pretty damaging, and the main problem to anyone not used to Jude is healing. Don't use Healer; Ivar's too fast for that. He'll also Seal your artes, get behind you, and break your guard. Seal Ward isn't a bad item! Keep dodging his combos, and try to free run and bait him into attacking air. He will attack faster than you; don't try to out speed him. Demon Fist can be used from a distance, but don't overdo it.

Jude's Snap Pivot, activated by backstepping away from an enemy's attack, is actually quite a nice ability as it gets him behind the enemy. It makes things a looooot easier. If you don't have it mastered, the battle is simple enough that it can be done without, but it will be harder.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Drop''     |
|c     700 |c     1000 |c [[Lavender]] |
+
|c ''' If you need additional help, watch this boss fight on YouTube using the link below, or through the embedded video above! ''' |
|c ''  http://youtu.be/mpAre9KXTDw                                                                                               '' |

====BOSS BATTLE #06 ====
@r|XNlIhgsfR60
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Hammerzamm (1)]]'''''                                        '''(LV. 22)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   6300 |c       518 |c       445 |c       409 |c       419 |
|c ''Normal''             |c   9000 |c       740 |c       636 |c       586 |c       600 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  13500 |c       888 |c       763 |c       702 |c       719 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  22500 |c      1111 |c       955 |c       879 |c       900 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  36000 |c      1481 |c      1273 |c      1172 |c      1201 |

This one has a spray attack and burrows underground to attack, but isn't particularly fast or hard hitting. However, when you get his HP down to a certain point, he does have a fairly fast underground attack that keeps following you; backstep from it. Jude has a variety of good linked artes with Leia, but Pixie Heal is particularly useful. Annoyingly, this guy will summon Worm Shades. Don't divert your attention to them; big guy will cause you more problems than a spell every so often. On higher difficulties, Arteseal is an annoyance.

It would not be a bad idea to knock him down (and again in the next battle!) for that stealable item.

|c ''EXP''    |c ''Gald''    |c ''Dropped Items''                  |c ''Stealable Items'' |
|c        800 |c        1200 |c [[Heavy Treat]], [[Specific Plus]] |c [[Seal Ward]]       |

But wait, there's more!

|*+6 '''''[[Hammerzamm (2)]]'''''                                        '''(LV. 22)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  15400 |c       647 |c       556 |c       512 |c       524 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  22000 |c       926 |c       795 |c       733 |c       751 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  33000 |c      1110 |c       954 |c       879 |c       900 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  55000 |c      1389 |c      1193 |c      1099 |c      1127 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  88000 |c      1852 |c      1501 |c      1466 |c      1502 |

Those items he just dropped should come in handy.

He hits harder this time, and has more than double the HP. Not to mention he inflicts Arteseal! Have someone equip Seal Charm, and everyone else can have a Seal Ward. Don't link with Leia except for stealing and the very occasional linked arte; she'll back off and heal if she isn't attached to you, and the battle will go more smoothly. The major thing to watch out for is that he sometimes lunges forward, instead of up, when underground. He also likes to stun a lot and even grab you like the smaller worms. Toward the end, he'll get ridiculously fast with going underground, then he'll start causing rocks to fall. And yes, he'll summon a worm again.

====BOSS BATTLE #07 ====
@r|2_aeQiKIY8s
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Brutaur]]'''''                                               '''(LV. 24)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  19600 |c       785 |c       704 |c       750 |c       629 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  28000 |c      1123 |c      1008 |c      1074 |c       899 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  42000 |c      1346 |c      1209 |c      1288 |c      1079 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  70000 |c      1684 |c      1511 |c      1611 |c      1349 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 112000 |c      2246 |c      2016 |c      2148 |c      1799 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |

Be careful to not get trapped against the edge, or in front of his charge; if you aren't guarding, you'll probably die. One of the more annoying things he does is summon the local monsters to assist him. If you have subpar equipment, he's absolutely going to kill you. Even with the best you can get, he hits incredibly hard, so block or die. There's no fast or easy way; bring a lot of items. He's also capable of stunning and inflicting Linkseal, as well as digging underground to attack you (backstep away from that one). As he dies, he'll rampage around and call a bunch of enemies. Obnoxious, but can be dealt with.

|c ''Hard''               |c  55000 |c      1740 |c      1643 |c      2341 |c      1951 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  88000 |c      2354 |c      2224 |c      3139 |c      2602 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Fire                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Water                                                     |

Presa is capable of throwing stuff at you (it stuns!) and casting artes. Stay on her; the AI cannot be relied upon to prevent her from casting artes, so they're better off occupying Wingul. Avoid getting close to both of them; one will shred you while the other will use that time to cast artes. It's impossible to leave the trap once in it. Separate, they're easy. Together, you're probably dead. And they will come together, like your own AI allies do, to protect each other, so you're just going to have to find a way to survive during those moments.

On higher difficulties, they may confuse you. Definitely the most obnoxious of ailments. Wingul also tends to like casting Arrivederci and Flame Ring. His spells are much less deadly than Presa's; they're more of an annoyance.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items''                 |c ''Stealable Items''                           |

====BOSS BATTLE #10 ====
@r|UhMnjtwKnIc
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Pterobronc]]'''''                                            '''(LV. 32)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  25200 |c      1135 |c       762 |c      1131 |c       720 |

|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |

A very mobile boss; hard to keep hitting. Obnoxiously, it spins to attack a very wide range which can keep staggering you, over and over. It's possible to get inside the attack radius so he can't hit you, though. It can also inflict you with Curse with its beam of darkness attack, along with Paralysis from another attack. Elize's Dispel is invaluable (if you don't have it, use the Jude/Elize Recover Heal). Since it's weak to water, Rowen isn't a bad choice for his Splash and Blue Sphere, as well as for Spash Beam (Rowen/Jude). Later in the fight, it starts to use fireballs and whirlwinds.

Overall, not a difficult boss. Just hard to keep in one place except with knockdown attacks.

====BOSS BATTLE #11 ====
@r|CCRJG_kwbcA
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Agria (1)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 33)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  21000 |c       702 |c       597 |c       591 |c       556 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  30000 |c      1176 |c      1026 |c      1102 |c      1010 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  45000 |c      1491 |c      1310 |c      1442 |c      1312 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  75000 |c      1964 |c      1738 |c      1953 |c      1765 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 120000 |c      2752 |c      2452 |c      2804 |c      2520 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Fire                                                      |

Strangely low stats, for a boss, and she has an odd obsession with using Lemon Gels (steal it to make her stop).

But! She'll throw the first Mystic Arte of the game on you, which will harm the entire party (maybe even kill someone, if you're unlucky). Don't be afraid to use a Treat after it... and bring out Elize, if you haven't, so she can Dispel and protect against Burn. If you see her overlimit, run. Your linked partner will follow you, at least, and she'll hopefully chase you through her entire overlimit instead of unleashing a Mystic Arte. The reason for this is because, to unleash a Mystic Arte, an Arcane Arte must connect with its target first. This applies to both you and the enemy.

As she dies, she'll spam a fire attack that hits a small area around her; it's hard to get a hit in if you stay too close to her. Mystic Arte aside, she's generally a pushover.

====BOSS BATTLE #12 ====
@r|SVRFzFwo9Rw
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Nachtigal]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 36)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  28000 |c      1501 |c      1536 |c      1148 |c      1102 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  40000 |c      2059 |c      2109 |c      1642 |c      1576 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  60000 |c      2430 |c      2490 |c      1969 |c      1891 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 100000 |c      2989 |c      3064 |c      2463 |c      2364 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 160000 |c      3918 |c      4019 |c      3284 |c      3152 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Water, Earth                                              |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

You have a Dark Cape from this very dungeon; equip it on whoever you think needs it the most. Also, you can steal an Amethyst from him, which you ought to equip immediately. He really likes darkness.

One of the things he likes to do is impale and toss you to the ground. He's also capable of cursing you, so, like always, Elize is a good idea. It's also a good idea to have at least one caster in the back, that way your party isn't taken out all at once.

At times, he'll change his blade to one emanating darkness, and his attacks will pack more of a punch. Then, when he's in overlimit, he'll try spamming Tyrant Spear to try and hit you with his Mystic Arte. STAY. BACK. Luckily, this doesn't hit everyone; just whoever happens to be in reach -- but beware, if everyone is in front of him, they're all as good as dead. (Drache only had Leia survive once. Guess who had the Amethyst equipped.) If everyone gets bunched together, RUN. That should get your linked partner to follow you, at least, which will spare part of your team from potential annihilation. Make sure to set the strategies to keep your frail allies away.

He can cast some artes; if you're ready for them, you can simply run out of their range. He can also stab his sword into the ground; while that attack can follow you, it's fairly easy to also run away from.

|*+6 '''''[[Jiao (2)]]'''''                                              '''(LV. 38)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  21000 |c      1300 |c      1158 |c       765 |c       818 |

Finally, a true three on four battle. Don't overuse casters; you want one caster (probably Elize for healing) and three people to be (mostly) bait. The problem with casters is that they'll probably be targeted in the middle of casting, making them useless. Focus on Jiao; he's definitely the most dangerous and the most obnoxious. He is capable of healing, somehow, so you'll need to seriously use your best wind attacks toward the end.

Note that these people can link. When one overlimits, the other can Mystic Arte away, so try to stay on the unlinked one and let the AI get murdered instead. And if one overlimits alone... again, let the AI be murdered. Fairy Circle (Milla/Elize and Milla/Leia) is actually quite helpful, as it whittles down Jiao's health and keeps up your own. But you're stuck in place, so beware using it.

The worst part? They can confuse you. Try to keep Dispel up. (That arte is simply divine. Elize is always welcome to the party.)

Try to spam your own Mystic Artes in this battle; you need to be in overlimit, then use an Arcane Arte (you probably only have a few, at this point) and holds X. They're increasingly going to go into Overlimit as they die; be patient, don't rush, and you can survive the Mystic Arte hell.

...And now a light based boss with a crap ton of attack. He has some lovely beam attacks, as well as one that wraps around him. He also likes Beast, which knocks you down, and multi-hit sword attacks. Like other bosses, he'll use Mystic Artes, and thus you should RUUUUN when he overlimits. He only hits the people in range, but it will kill whoever gets caught. As he dies, his attacks get crazier, and he starts to confuse you (jerk!).

Be patient; guard when you have to, try to only use life bottles for your main and best healer, and only approach when it's relatively safe. This battle is something of a slog, or maybe even a war of attrition, but only because he hits hard.

====BOSS BATTLE #17 ====
@r|k5_22jsGxqE
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Alvin]]'''''                                                 '''(LV. 48)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c   9800 |c      1117 |c      1272 |c      1253 |c      1203 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  14000 |c      1640 |c      1819 |c      1792 |c      1720 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  21000 |c      1988 |c      2182 |c      2149 |c      2062 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  35000 |c      2510 |c      2729 |c      2688 |c      2580 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  56000 |c      3381 |c      3639 |c      3584 |c      3440 |

You can equip a Reverse Doll, which you should have gotten in the previous dungeon. Alternatively, there's Black Onyx, Amulet (burn sucks), or Stun Talisman. Black Onyx is probably the least useful, but it can help you out of a pinch. Alternatively, you can try Stun Bracelet and Syrup Bottle together, and only equip the Reverse Doll or Black Onyx when you get caught in a combo or a tough spot.

Be warned -- he hits like a TRUCK. You will need to abuse free run and snap pivot if you want to survive. Try to free run around shots (if you see them coming) and snap pivot his sword swings. You can also approach him after he finishes attacking, but be careful. Use a knockdown attack, such as Beast, if you need to heal up. Ideally, don't get hit. Seriously, one of his combos can bring you down. Do use Steel; every bit of attack will help.

Toward the end, he'll heal himself using Guardian Field. Once he starts pulling that, consider spamming Demon Fist to prevent him from getting a full heal out of it.

====BOSS BATTLE #18-J ====
@r|7ETrIFw2jMk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (1)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 50)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |

You'll want Leia and Jude (or just Jude!) up front, so Rowen and Elize can hang back and do what they do best.

Muzet hits pretty hard, including behind her, so you will take quite the beating. You should be a little patient when approaching her, or else don't constantly link with a partner so they don't keep trying (and failing) to match your movements.

She also looooves ailments, so keep Dispel up. Her darkness spells tend to hold you in place or draw you in, so do your best to stay clear of those.

Once she overlimits, she'll spam long range magic suddenly... Block the stuff that follows you, if you can't run around it in time, and run away from any spells. One of your allies is sure to be dumb enough to get hit by her Mystic Arte, so keep your health way up, and use whatever you need to survive.

====BOSS BATTLE #18-M ====
@r|HOansGUaDeI
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (2)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 50)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  14700 |c      1469 |c      1375 |c      1565 |c      1473 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  21000 |c      2101 |c      1966 |c      2238 |c      2107 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  31500 |c      2520 |c      2358 |c      2684 |c      2527 |
|c ''Hard''               |c  52500 |c      3151 |c      2950 |c      3357 |c      3160 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c  84000 |c      4202 |c      3933 |c      4476 |c      4214 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Light                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

You should have a Rebirth Doll from the Zenethra. If you feel like you're going to die, equip it. Black Onyx can also be used if you get snagged in a combo, but it's less reliable since it only increases your HP.

She capable of many status ailments, so use Syrup Bottles or an Amulet. If you back off of her, she'll attempt to attack you from underground or cast a wind/dark/fire spell. The Four, naturally, are good attacks to use once you start staggering her, as well as any light attacks you have (Drache used Divine Streak; do spam it if you're in a tight spot, it's wonderful). The best way to handle her is hit and run... or guard, but be careful, as she can break it fairly easily. She can throw you, regardless of whether you're guarding, and she can attack in all directions. Once she overlimits, she'll spam long range magic suddenly... Block the stuff that follows you, if you can't run from it in time, and run away from any spells. Her Mystic Arte will reduce you to 1 HP. Avoid the black ball; it holds you in place. The black things on the ground also draw you to them, so stay far away.

The major problem with her is that a couple combos may be enough to kill you. The easiest times to attack her are after she tries her underground stabby attack, when she taunts you, and when she passes through you. If you're close enough, you should be able to nail her before she casts a spell too. You can also try knocking her down with a Flare Bomb if you need a short breather.

====BOSS BATTLE #21 ====
@r|mnFmWnVVNpI
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Maxwell]]'''''                                               '''(LV. 60)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  49000 |c      2724 |c      2044 |c      2324 |c      2212 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  70000 |c      3720 |c      2920 |c      3320 |c      3160 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c 105000 |c      4384 |c      3504 |c      3984 |c      3792 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 175000 |c      5380 |c      4380 |c      4980 |c      4740 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 280000 |c      7040 |c      5840 |c      6640 |c      6320 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Variable; opposite of strength                            |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Variable                                                  |

Coming from Jude's side, a scene will happen a little into the battle, then another after his Mystic Arte, and yet another after a second one! Theeeennnn the party really starts. And the butthole's HP is reset.

He's a little hard to knock down and has big attacks. You'll notice Maxwell uses variations of attacks Milla has, so you should generally know what his attacks do; knockdown from fire, hold in place with darkness, and so on. The biggest problem is that the jerkface steals your TP, so you may want to use Treats. His Mystic Arte will hit the entire party, but it isn't devastating (especially with all elemental resistances up).  He's really not that difficult and should go down fairly easily.

The great thing about Milla is that she hits about every weakness, making her great for this battle... not to mention the Four are quite broken, if costly.

====BOSS BATTLE #25 ====
@r|zOAr5J8c4sk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Gaius (3)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 70)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  84000 |c      1812 |c      1873 |c      2142 |c      1261 |
|c ''Normal''             |c 120000 |c      3233 |c      3190 |c      3275 |c      2317 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c 180000 |c      4179 |c      4068 |c      4030 |c      3020 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 300000 |c      5599 |c      5385 |c      5162 |c      4075 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 480000 |c      7966 |c      7581 |c      7050 |c      5834 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Dark                                                      |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Light                                                     |
|*+6 '''''[[Muzet (4)]]'''''                                             '''(LV. 70)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  37800 |c      1535 |c      1397 |c      1392 |c      1584 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  54000 |c      2751 |c      2511 |c      2633 |c      2777 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  81000 |c      3561 |c      3253 |c      3458 |c      3573 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 135000 |c      4777 |c      4366 |c      4699 |c      4766 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 216000 |c      6802 |c      6222 |c      6766 |c      6755 |
|c ''Weaknesses''         |+5 Light                                                     |
|c ''Strengths''          |+5 Dark                                                      |

Together, they'll mow you over; rely on your cheapest tactics possible -- running! Gradually, your party will rejoin and use their Mystic Artes. Just focus on surviving till you get a full party.

Like for other bosses, you can abuse elemental resistances. Start out with Amethyst, Elemental, Diamond, and such, as well as your best armor that resists either Light/Dark. Don't pull out Red/Blue Cape till one of them is gone. Beware: Muzet casts Sunburst.

Note that Muzet's health is a LOT lower. But it's hard to beat her down; she'll auto-revive once in the battle, and that's if she doesn't otherwise heal up first. Apparently she heals when she guards, so make sure to break it using Beast or something. Consider using an Hourglass if you have too much trouble with her. Otherwise, Muzet's not really all that different from the other times you fought her; she's more tedious than difficult.

Do not beat Gaius first; Muzet can revive him to half health. Put EVERYTHING into taking Muzet down.

One thing they're capable of is stopping time (like an Hourglass), then pummeling you. Do your best to not get right between them; they'll rip you apart. Gaius is good at shredding, but he's actually not too bad till he gets super-fast at the halfway point. At this point, Elize should have Revive and Leia should have good item skills, so use them both as necessary.

Oh yes. Do STEAL from both of them so they can't use their items. Muzet is particularly obnoxious with Treat spamming.

====Golden Mage Knight====
@r|L4Gy2xpqawk
=-----=
|*+6 '''''[[Golden Mage Knight - Mercenary]]'''''                        '''(LV. 80)''' |
|                         |c ''HP'' |c ''P.ATK'' |c ''P.DEF'' |c ''A.ATK'' |c ''A.DEF'' |
|c ''Easy''               |c  63000 |c      5143 |c      2938 |c      3711 |c      2134 |

|c ''Unknown''            |c 360000 |c      9999 |c      9323 |c      8750 |c      7030 |

This guy is POWERFUL, since he's an Alvin clone. Especially if you didn't grind and you're ten levels below him! :D He can wipe out some of the weaker characters in a few hits, so beware who you take into battle. The cheap (and recommended) way is to use Elize's Revive on everyone so you don't constantly have to use resurrection spells/items. Really, you need to conserve your items for the last part of this fight.

Any fire resistance you can get is a good thing here. Even if you need to move your armor down a couple tiers. It will help. Equip Red Capes, if you need to. Phoenix Ribbon, Dragon Helm, Garnet, and so on are good alternatives when combined with other Fire resisting equipment.

|c ''Easy''               |c  44800 |c      4113 |c      2415 |c      5433 |c      3597 |
|c ''Normal''             |c  64000 |c      5447 |c      3666 |c      7334 |c      5353 |
|c ''Moderate''           |c  96000 |c      6337 |c      4498 |c      8601 |c      6524 |
|c ''Hard''               |c 160000 |c      7671 |c      5749 |c      9999 |c      8280 |
|c ''Unknown''            |c 256000 |c      9895 |c      7832 |c      9999 |c      9999 |

Yeeeeep. Two casters now; Puppeteer and Creator. This is going to hurt. The last one, you could have done okay in. This one? People are going to die. There's just no way around it. Milla's spirits are even better here, as they create a fine excuse to attack her over other targets.

The Puppeteer is the worst, though, as it heals and casts. Be prepared to kick its ass quickly. Once it goes down (it will be difficult due to HP fluctuations), the battle will go smoothly. Beast is effective at stopping Healing Circle.

You can take down the Creator first, if you want, but only do so if you have enough Dark resist on everyone so the Puppeteer can be totally ineffective... except for Terror and occasional healing. Otherwise, resist light instead of darkness.

Save the Scholar for last; he hits REALLY hard, and you don't need that on top of the Creator's spells.

Elements... pretty much any resistances would be useful. Puppeteer loves darkness, and the Creator likes to spam everything but water.

|c ''EXP'' |c ''Gald'' |c ''Dropped Items''                                    |c ''Stealable Items''                                                               |
|c  120000 |c        0 |c [[Blue Saffron]], [[Blue Chamomile]], [[Blue Basil]] |c [[Red Saffron]] (Scholar), [[Red Chamomile]] (Creator), [[Red Basil]] (Puppeteer) |

====Jude's Artes====
%

====Healer====
|* TP Cost |* Attribute |
|c       5 |c PSY       |

%

|* TP Cost |
|c      13 |

===Consumables===

====Apple Gel====
* Restores 30% HP. The taste of apple you know and love! One of two staples for any journey.
** Dropped by: [[Boar]], [[Bat]], [[Sword Bee]], [[Fennmont Sentry]]
** Stolen from: [[Sol Cat]], [[Hawk]], [[Spyrix Warrior 2]]

%

====Lemon Gel====
* Restores 60% HP. Has a lemony flavor and smells of tasty citrus!
** Dropped by: [[Stalwart Elite]], [[Prickle Spider (Spirit Realm)]], [[Sylvan Mare (Spirit Realm)]], [[Rashugal Battlecorps Officer]]
** Stolen from: [[Agria (1)]], [[Rashugal Battlecorps Deserter]], [[Insurgent Soldier]], [[Auj Oule Royal Guard]]

%

====Orange Gel====
* Restores 30% TP. Loaded with orange flavor! Another one of two staples for any journey.
** Dropped by: [[Prickle Spider]], [[Insect Plant]], [[Spirit Artes Researcher]], [[Rashugal Spiritcorps Channeler]]
** Stolen from: [[Treant]], [[Spirit Artes Researcher]], [[Green Butterfly]], [[Filifreet]]

%

====Pineapple Gel====
* Restores 60% TP. It's like there's a tropical party in your mouth, and everyone's invited!
** Dropped by: [[Axe Beak (Spirit Realm)]], [[Merfish (Spirit Realm)]], [[Insect Plant (Spirit Realm)]], [[Wolf (Spirit Realm)]]
** Stolen from: [[Terra Treant]], [[Rock Djinn]]

%

====Melange Gel====
* Restores 30% HP and TP. The ingredients and ratios for the mix are an industry secret!
** Dropped by: [[Stalwart Commander]], [[Mighty Plant]], [[Bog Plant]], [[Infiltrator Captain]]
** Stolen from: [[Harpy]]

%

====Miracle Gel====
* Restores 60% HP and TP. Miraculous ingredients, miraculous taste. Hallelujah!
** Dropped by: [[Treant (Spirit Realm)]], [[Bacura]], [[Bronze Bacura]], [[Silver Bacura]]
** Stolen from: [[Stalwart Commander]], [[Lizardman]], [[Tiny Teagle]], [[Tree Crab]]

%

====Treat====
* Restores 30% of the party's HP. A somewhat pricy remedy.
** Dropped by: [[Stalwart Sergeant]], [[Armored Boar]], [[Sentinel Spider]], [[Magma Scorpion]]
** Stolen from: [[Stalwart Elite]], [[Water Djinn]], [[Fire Djinn]], [[Wind Element]]

%

====Heavy Treat====
* Restores 60% of the party's HP. An extremely pricy remedy.
** Dropped by: [[Hammerzamm (1)]]
** Stolen from: [[Muzet (4)]], [[Veywind Eye]], [[Stalwart Sergeant]], [[Tetra Djinn]]

%

====Specific====
* Restores 30% of the party's TP. A special remedy that works in a pinch!
** Dropped by: [[Lizitar]], [[Infiltrator Sergeant]], [[Infiltrator Commander]], [[Snow Wolf]]
** Stolen from: [[Infiltrator Captain]], [[Snow Tortoise]], [[Auj Oule Spy]], [[Technician Commander]]

%

====Specific Plus====
* Restores 60% of the party's TP. It doesn't come cheap!
** Dropped by: [[Hammerzamm (1)]]
** Stolen from: [[Graddic Claw]], [[Lizitar]], [[Infiltrator Sergeant]], [[Infiltrator Commander]]

%

====Elixir====
* Fully restores HP & TP, cures KO, and all status abnormalities. A spiritual medicine which gives eternal life.
** Dropped by: [[Megistus Harpy]], [[Technician Sergeant]]
** Stolen from: [[Technician Sergeant]], [[Burrow Goblin]]

%

====Omega Elixir====
* Fully restores HP & TP, cures KO, and all status abnormalities for the entire party. A miraculous medicine.
** Dropped by: [[Temporal Sentinel]]
** Stolen from: [[Gaius (3)]], [[Volt]], [[Fire Teagle]]

%

====Life Bottle====
* Cures KO and restores 30% HP and 15% TP at the time of revival.
** Dropped by: [[Antler Beak]], [[Bladed Boar]], [[Lizardman]], [[Exodus Infiltrator]]
** Stolen from: [[Stalwart Captain]], [[Merfish]], [[Spider]], [[Penguinist]]

%

====Panacea Bottle====
* Heals all physical and magical ailments. Highly useful in battle.
** Dropped by: [[Axe Beak (Spirit Realm)]], [[Snowmelt Merfish]], [[Quag Merfish]], [[Sylvan Treant]]
** Stolen from: [[Exodus Infiltrator]], [[Terra Goblin]], [[Skunky]]

%

====Syrup Bottle====
* Prevents all physical and magical ailments. An all-purpose medicine that's highly useful on the battlefield.
** Dropped by: [[Exodus Stalwart]], [[Frost Beak]], [[Lizardman]], [[Scorpion]]

%

====Holy Bottle====
* Allows you to avoid encounters with weaker enemies for a time. A mysterious liquid imbued with holy energy.
** Dropped by: [[Fleet Mare (Spirit Realm)]], [[Snow Bat]], [[Gun Bee]], [[Ice Mandragora]]

%

====Dark Bottle====
* For a time, enemies will become more aggressive and encounter you frequently. A dark and mysterious liquid.
** Dropped by: [[Fire Bat]], [[Mechanical Golem]], [[Earth Golem]], [[Frost Skeleton]]

%

====Ice Pop====
* Restores 10% HP. If you get a Win Stick, you get another for free!

%

====Win Stick====
* A lucky win for an Ice Pop. You can bring it to the snack bar and get another one for free!

%

====Lose Stick====
* An unfortunate loss found in an Ice Pop. Bring it back to the snack bar and get a whole lot of nothing. Losing sure sucks!

%

====All-Divide====
* Cuts damage for allies and enemies by 50%. Use it again to return damage to normal. How mysterious!
** Stolen from: [[Megistus Harpy]]

%

====Hourglass====
* Stops enemies for a fixed period of time. A mystical item that can turn the tables on a sticky situation!
** Dropped by: [[Megistus Mandragora]]

%

====Sage====
* Increases max HP by 10. An herb used for tea since ancient times.

%

====Savory====
* Increases max TP by 10. When cooked with beans, it adds a rather "savory" taste indeed!

%

%

====Verbena====

** Dropped by: [[Gentlesylph]]

%

====Chamomile====

** Dropped by: [[Spyrix Warrior 3]], [[Gentlemundine]]

%

====Basil====

** Dropped by: [[Spyrix Warrior 2]]

%
====Saffron====
* Increases AGI by 1. This herb is also used frequently as a yellow dye.
** Dropped by: [[Gentlegnome]]

%

====Jasmine====
* Increases DEX by 1. This herb is widely grown for use as a tea and for decoration.

===Valuables===

====Item Book====
* A catalog of all items found. It also records which enemies drop the item and which enemies it can be stolen from.

%

====Enemy Book====
* A catalog of all enemies and monsters encountered. It also records data such as enemy weaknesses.

%

====Battle Book====
* A list of combat tutorials. Refer to this whenever you forget the controls.

%

====World Map====

* A world map that records all of the places you've visited.

%

====Item Sphere====
* An item that allows you to change Auto-Items settings in the Strategy menu.

%

====Item Sphere Plus====
* An item that increases the number of slots in your Auto-Items menu. Each Item Sphere Plus adds another slot.

%

====Artes Sphere====
* An item that allows you to set up to sixteen artes.

%

====Winged Boots====
* With these mysterious boots, your running speed increases while exploring the world.
** Dropped by: [[Nameless Anomaly]]

%

====Class Credit Form====
* Documentation that allows a Talim Medical School resident to earn credit for on-site medical training.

%

====Research Center Key====
* A strangely-shaped key used at the Laforte Research Center.

%

====Kresnik Key====
* A key developed at the Laforte Research Center to activate the Lance of Kresnik.

%

====Temporal Earth Stone====
* An earth-element medium that acts as a conduit between the human realm and the spirit realm.

%

====Temporal Water Stone====
* A water-element medium that acts as a conduit between the human realm and the spirit realm.

%

====Temporal Fire Stone====
* A fire-element medium that acts as a conduit between the human realm and the spirit realm.

%

====Temporal Wind Stone====
* A wind-element medium that acts as a conduit between the human realm and the spirit realm.

%

====Milla's Pendant====
* A glass bead pendant made for Milla back in Sharilton.

%

====Elevator Key====
* A card key used to activate the elevators in Fort Gandala.

%

====Control Room Key====
* A key needed to enter the control room in Fort Gandala.

%

====Miner's Kit====
* A complete set of mining tools that was snuck out of Leia's dad's room.

%

====Aspyrixis (1)====
* A mysterious medical contraption found in the archives of the Mathis Clinic.

%

====Aspyrixis (2)====
* A mysterious medical contraption set with a mana-containing spirit fossil.

%

====Leia's Notes====
* Notes that catalog Leia's reasons for joining in the party's journey. Their contents are known only to Leia and Milla.

%

====Booster====
* A device manufactured in Auj Oule that forcefully amplifies the mana secreted by one's mana lobe.

%

====Radio====
* An Elympion device carried by a soldier on the Zenethra.

%

====Zenethra Map====
* A map of the ship carried by a soldier on the Zenethra.

%

====Father's Memento====
* A gun that Alvin's father treasured. It had been in Gilland's possession for many years.

%

====Soul's Light====
* An arte in which the information from Milla's soul has been recorded. It was received from Maxwell's specter.

%

====Spyrix Casing====
* A casing with its spirit fossil removed. It can also serve to control spirit fossils.

%

====Muzet's Knife====
* A physical manifestation of Muzet's ability to cut through space-time.

%

====Spirit Fossil Husk====
* The fossil of a spirit that was drained by a spyrix. Since it no longer contains mana, it is referred to as a husk.

%

====Spirit Clime Examination Arte====
* Documents outlining a special type of spirit arte.

%

====Golem Inhibitor====
* A special device that changes the spirit clime in order to lower the defensive power of golems.

%

====Gun Belt====
* By carrying this item, Alvin learns the Charge Armor skill.

%

====Light-leaf Clover====
* A clover that shines like the sun, said to have gone extinct more than a decade ago.

%

====Long Dau Dictionary====
* A dictionary used for translating the language of Auj Oule's Long Dau clan.

%

====Package Addressed to Inn====
* A sealed package small enough to carry under one arm.

%

====Lucky Charm====
* A charm created by a young girl for her father.

%

====Ex-Miner's Wine====
* A bottle of wine.

%

====Rare Vase====
* A suspicious-looking vase with Efreet's hallmark.

%

====Letter to Father====
* A letter addressed by a woman to her father.

%

====Napple====
* A red fruit that is a famous export of Hamil. Known for its perfect balance of sweet and sour flavors.

%

====Porange====
* A famous Hamil export also known as "candle fruit". It is also used to make wine.

%

====Golden Key====
* A brilliant golden key that opens the door to Magnus Zero.

%

====Arte Tome: "One-Hit Kill"====
* A tome that grants Jude access to the Blunt Fang martial arte.
** Dropped by: [[Crimson Servant]]

%

====Arte Tome: "Tremorous Fist"====
* A tome that grants Jude access to the Shattering Demon Fist arcane arte.

%

====Arte Tome: "Spirit Surge"====
* A tome that grants Milla access to the Overdrive arcane arte.

%

====Skill Tome: "Pinprick"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the Minimum Damage skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Soul Dividend"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the EXP Share skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Vigor Shared"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the Linked Action skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Joyful Gains"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the Happiness skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Widened Limits"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the Sustain Limit skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Absolute Defense"====
* A tome that grants the party access to the Impregnable Guard skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "One with Beauty"====
* A tome that grants Jude access to the Milla sync skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Indefatigable"====
* A tome that grants Jude access to the Grounded Stance skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "One with Youth"====
* A tome that grants Milla access to the Jude Sync skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Wall of Soul"====
* A tome that grants Milla access to the Energy Barrier skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Tetra Infusion"====

%

====Skill Tome: "Death Defiance"====
* A tome that grants Elize access to the Survive skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Gifted Healer"====
* A tome that grants Elize access to the Healer's Reward skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Spirit Negation"====
* A tome that grants Rowen access to the Anti-Magic skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Flash Casting"====
* A tome that grants Rowen access to the Tetra Spell skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Gift of Life"====
* A tome that grants Leia access to the Self-Sacrifice skill.

%

====Skill Tome: "Warrior Above"====
* A tome that grants Leia access to the Sky Soldier skill.

%

====Mysterious Jewel====
* A jewel that possesses a mysterious beauty. Its purpose is completely unclear.
** Dropped by: [[Veywind Eye]], [[Graddic Claw]]

%

====Jet Black Feather====
* Black feathers that can be found throughout the world. No one is sure what sort of creature sheds them.

====Jet Black Feathers====
=-----=
* ''Location:'' Sharilton - East Market
* ''When:'' Chapter 1: Upon arriving at Sharilton
* ''Reward:'' [[Accel]], 50000 gald
* ''Description:'' Exchange feathers for items. See [[Jet Black Feather Trading Post]] for the selection. Give 459 feathers for a scene in which you have to chase him down to Culmar Trail.

|* Reward                                   |* Feathers Given |
| [[Artes Sphere]], 10000 gald              |             100 |
| [[Hat]], [[Hat Style (Jude)]], [[Hat Style (Milla)]], [[Hat Style (Alvin)]], [[Hat Style (Elize)]], [[Hat Style (Rowen)]], [[Hat Style (Leia)]], 20000 gald |             200 |
| [[Blue Sephira]], 30000 gald              |             300 |
| [[Classy Lady Garb (Milla)]], [[Casual Outfit (Alvin)]], 40000 gald  |             400 |

=-=

==FAQ (Frequently Asked Questions)==

:'''''What are the major differences between playing as Jude and Milla?'''''
*** The majority of the game is the same. However, there are quite a few differences.
**** The game starts a bit differently depending on who you choose; Jude has the ability to explore Fennmont before Milla joins.
**** A few sub events differ, in content and in deadlines. Each side also has a couple unique sub events.
**** There are points in the game where the one you choose will be separated from the other, and you'll have to go through different dungeons.
**** Each character has access to a few monsters and bosses that the other does not.
**** Each character has exclusive cut scenes that the other does not.
**** The dialogue with NPC's is different.
**** Some of the storyline is revealed a bit differently depending on the perspective.
**** Jude and Milla each have their own set of battle themes. (We like Jude's a bit better.)
+
+
:'''''What are the differences between Manual, Semi-Auto, and Auto?'''''
*** Manual gives you full control on everything, meaning you control the direction, range, and aim of your attacks/artes as well.
*** Semi-Auto helps you out and automatically changes your direction, range, and aim so that your attacks/artes can actually hit the enemy without much interaction. It also helps you automatically guard at times.
*** Auto is having your character controlled automatically by the AI, like your party members. You do nothing.

+

+
